As for the Japanese troops at Tongwen Academy, Huafeng, Gongda, Toyota, and the yarn factories, there are currently only ten to dozens of people at each place, and the Japanese side will also withdraw them soon.

Guo Taiqi Discusses Diplomacy 112

Resumption of Diplomatic Relations with Russia and the Roundtable Conference

Regarding the issue of resuming diplomatic relations with Russia and the Roundtable Conference, there has been much discussion recently. Although the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has repeatedly expressed its views, people outside the ministry are still confused. A reporter from Huadong News Agency specially visited Mr. Guo at his residence yesterday morning to inquire in detail about the overall views of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the above two issues. According to Mr. Guo, regarding the resumption of diplomatic relations with Russia, when he was in Beijing, he held a Foreign Affairs Committee meeting at the residence of Executive Yuan President Wang Jingwei to discuss this matter specifically. Although most parties agreed to the resumption of diplomatic relations, considering the importance of the matter, it should be handled with utmost caution. Therefore, it was transferred to the Central Political Conference for discussion, and the Central Committee has also discussed it several times, but has not yet decided on a specific plan. However, it is firmly believed that a definite plan will be available within a short period of time. In his opinion, our country and Russia are closely adjacent and have a very long history. It is not a proper solution to cut off diplomatic relations for a long time, and both countries, government and public, are eager for the trend of resuming diplomatic relations. As long as the differences and regulations in political and economic aspects can be fully restricted and stipulated, the resumption of diplomatic relations will be very easy. The UK and France have also discussed and decided on resuming diplomatic relations with Russia several times. Our country, especially at this time when the communist bandits are rampant across the country, should strive for prudence. As for the roundtable conference that Japan is touting, it is obvious that this is a political trick by the Japanese government to deal with its own people. Since the Japanese army's attack on Shanghai was unjustified and the defeated soldiers and lost generals ended up with nothing, they were not only abandoned by world opinion but also opposed by the people of the whole country. Therefore, they touted the fallacy of the roundtable conference and the Free City of Shanghai, hoping to use this trick to shift the resentment of the Japanese people in the past and to cater to the psychology of ignorant people in various countries. As for the Free City, we can laugh it off. As for the roundtable conference, as long as it does not conflict with our position, we should be happy to promote its success. However, today, the Japanese side's opinion is not like this. They actually intend to separate the Northeast and Shanghai issues into two, and our side will definitely oppose this intention. The so-called roundtable conference is a meeting resolved by the League of Nations to resolve the entire Sino-Japanese negotiation issue. It is clearly stipulated that the Northeast Incident and the Shanghai Incident must be resolved as a whole in the conference. Today, the Japanese side does not plan this, hoping to resolve the Shanghai Incident and the Northeast Incident separately. For the Northeast Incident, they firmly declared that no third country is allowed to interfere, and their ambitions are blatantly revealed. Our country should vigorously oppose it. Therefore, as for the so-called roundtable conference, the Japanese side's attitude is like this, and the distance from our country's position is still far away. It seems too early at this time. Talking about this, the reporter then inquired about two things: (1) The Japanese side is publicizing that the Manchurian puppet state has sent two Japanese people to serve as deputy consuls in Russia. Is this statement reliable? Will this matter be an obstacle to the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia? (2) When will the Vice Minister go abroad? According to Mr. Guo: (1) Russia and the puppet state have no diplomatic relations to speak of. In fact, it is impossible for the puppet state to send consuls. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has not received a report on this matter. It should be a deliberate rumor by the Japanese side. (2) The time for his departure has not been determined.

City National Products Exhibition

Yesterday's Opening Ceremony 113

Unveiled by Army Commander Cai and other representatives

Open to the Public with Strict Security

The City Chamber of Commerce, in conjunction with four national products organizations, organized the Shanghai City National Products Exhibition, which held its opening ceremony at 10:00 AM yesterday. Minister Chen, Army Commander Cai, and Brigade Commander Weng acted as representatives to perform the unveiling ceremony. Security was very strict at the venue, and all participants were given a bag of national products. The details are recorded below.

Opening Ceremony of the National Products Exhibition (Photo by Li Zunyong) 114

Representatives Present: Central Committee Member Song Yuanyuan, Yang Jianping representing Minister of Transportation Chen Mingshu, Fan Qiwu representing Army Commander Cai of the 19th Route Army, He Bing of the Ministry of Industry, Chen Kecheng of Tang Chengdu South Government, Xu Huheng of the Police Headquarters, Zhu Yang of the Municipal Party Department, Ye Mujju of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Yu Tianbi of the Social Affairs Bureau, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Fang Jiaobo, and Wu Zhihao of the City Chamber of Commerce, Pei Yunqing of the Money Industry Association, Chen Shaofu of the Industrial Products Exhibition Hall of the Ministry of Industry, Hu Fengxiang of the City Federation, Zhang Yichen of the Trade Union Federation, Wang Jie'an of the China National Products Maintenance Association, Chen Yiting of the Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, Zhu Zhenhan of the Machine-Made National Products Factory Union, Lu Xingzhuang of the National Products Factory Union, and more than 1,000 representatives from various trade associations, labor unions, and public organizations.

Strict Security: Wang Xiaolai, Ye Huijun of the City Chamber of Commerce, Wang Jie'an of the National Products Maintenance Association, Chen Yiting of the Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, Zhu Zhenhan of the Machine-Made National Products Factory Union, and Lu Xingzhuang of the National Products Factory Union served as the presidium, with Yan E'sheng as secretary, Zheng Chengqing as general manager, Zhu Boyuan as master of ceremonies, Zhong Jinzhen as recorder, and Zhou Xiuquan, Zhang Bofang, Sun Choucheng, Zhu Dechao, etc. as receptionists. Zhang Zhongwu, captain of the Seventh Squadron of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, led three armed police officers, together with the entire Chamber of Commerce Security Team and the entire Boy Scouts, to maintain order at the venue. Security was very strict.

Unveiling Ceremony Details: At 10:00 AM yesterday, the opening ceremony was held in the City Chamber of Commerce Auditorium. The City Public Security Bureau Military Band played music first, followed by speeches by the chairman and representatives of various organizations. At 11:30 AM, everyone took a photo together as the music played, and the meeting adjourned. Chairman Wang Xiaolai accompanied the representative of Army Commander Cai to unveil the National Products Exhibition, while setting off firecrackers and raising the national flag for people to visit.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Wang Xiaolai reported that today, the Commodity Exhibition Hall of the Chamber, in conjunction with the four major national products organizations in the city, held the opening ceremony of the Shanghai City National Products Exhibition. He felt extremely honored to have received the guidance of all sectors of society. The Exhibition Hall of the Chamber was established in the tenth year of the Republic of China, which is eleven years ago. It gathers the essence of domestic products for reference by all sectors of society. In these eleven years, in addition to holding exhibitions and six temporary national products bazaars, it has been open daily for people to visit and promote national products. Furthermore, in March of last year, due to the influx of foreign goods into the market and the sluggish sales of national products, it was impossible to find a fully national products store in Shanghai, causing those who love to use national products to be at a loss. Considering that the previous Industrial and Commercial Conference had a resolution to reward the establishment of national products stores, and that national products exhibition halls in Nanjing, Hangzhou, and other places had already increased their numbers, it was urgent. Therefore, on the first floor of the Chamber, a permanent national products bazaar was opened, and national products factories were contacted to promote it together. After three months of preparation, it was finally completed. Since its opening, business has been quite good. It can be seen that our patriotic men and women are determined to use national products, and we are very grateful. The reason for reopening the exhibition this time is that after the January 28th Incident, national products factories in Zhabei were few due to the war. Fearing that it would be difficult to recover after the destruction, we hope to come back again. We hope that our patriotic people and compatriots across the country will not be lazy and will be encouraged again. The Chamber is in charge of promotion, so we are thinking about how to encourage and guide it. In the midst of discussions, on April 26th, we received a letter from the Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, stating that when manufacturers are tired, foreign goods can take advantage of the opportunity to enter, which is worrying, and asking us to design a plan to expand publicity and actively awaken the public with a common will and a spirit of cooperation. The Chamber believes that we have the same goals and cannot shirk our responsibility. After deliberation, we joined forces with the China National Products Maintenance Association, the Shanghai Citizens' National Products Promotion Association, the Shanghai Machine-Made National Products Factory Union, and the Shanghai National Products Factory Union to organize the Shanghai City National Products Exhibition, with the aim of encouraging production, consumption, supply, and demand, and guiding men, women, old and young. Although the scale is rough, there is room for improvement, and the equipment seeks to be comprehensive, hoping to attract people to national products. Therefore, we classify them by category and display them in the room, listing the prices and names to indicate the criteria. The purpose of the initiative is this. The 6th of this month happened to be the anniversary of the National Products Bazaar, so the Chamber opened it on this day for one month, and a sales department was set up in the exhibition on the second floor to sell cheap domestic products. We hope that patriotic men and women will come and visit enthusiastically and promote it, so that we can expand it and fill Shanghai, and the people's livelihood can be revived. After the exhibition is over, we plan to reorganize the national products bazaar on the second floor to make it permanent. Furthermore, we are honored to have Army Commander Cai Tingkai attend the meeting and perform the unveiling ceremony, and to have the representatives of the Ministry of Industry Tang Huoshu and Mr. Chen Kecheng of the Municipal Government, and Director Yu of the Social Affairs Bureau give speeches. The Chamber feels very honored and sincerely thanks them, and hopes that people from all walks of life will give criticisms and promote it widely, which is especially welcome.

Fan's Speech: Then, Fan Qiwu spoke on behalf of Army Commander Cai, saying, "Today, the Shanghai City National Products Exhibition is holding its opening ceremony. Army Commander Cai originally wanted to participate in person, but due to the busy affairs of the military department, he was unable to do so. Therefore, he sent me as a representative to participate in this National Products Exhibition. In my personal opinion, I believe that the Chinese people are happy to use and promote national products. The reason for this is that everyone loves themselves. Looking at all countries in the world, no matter which country, they all pay close attention to their own industry and commerce in order to develop and prosper. For example, the increase in tariffs is nothing more than to resist the influx of foreign goods and protect the sales of domestic goods. How should the production of domestic goods in our country be gradually developed in the future? In short, there are two points: (1) Entrepreneurs should do their best to invent and reform to increase production and improve products. (2) The people should especially like to use domestic goods and fully promote them to make them sell well. Although we know that the current products of our country cannot be compared with foreign goods, we should still take patriotism as a prerequisite and take wearing and using domestic goods as glory. We must know that the development of industry and commerce cannot be achieved in one day. Especially in our economically backward country, we should encourage ourselves and each other. Furthermore, a large part of the raw materials of the products in the national products stores are imported from foreign countries. Therefore, some people point out that they are not domestic goods, but this is too harsh. It is not known that the products of various countries are not necessarily all produced in their own countries. Therefore, we can only hope to gradually study and replace them with domestic products. If a kind of domestic product must be produced entirely in our own country before it can be considered a domestic product, it seems very difficult in fact. In short, to promote domestic goods, the government and the people must fully cooperate. The government is responsible for protection, and the people are responsible for promotion. Only then can the people be rich and the country be strong. It is not to say that the people are rich and the country is strong, and everything depends on military force. Finally, I hope that after the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce has done its best to promote it, the future of domestic goods will be improved day by day, so that it will not be in vain to hold today's grand event."

Speech by the Ministry of Industry: He Bingxian, Deputy Director of the International Trade Bureau, representing the Ministry of Industry, said, "Chairman and everyone, today is the opening day of the Shanghai City National Products Exhibition. I am very honored to be sent by the Ministry of Industry to participate as a representative. I just listened to Chairman Wang's report on the preparations, and I admire everyone's past efforts very much. Holding a National Products Exhibition is a very meaningful thing, especially at this time of national crisis, with the Northeast fallen and northern Shanghai destroyed, it has a more far-reaching meaning. Since September 18th of last year, when Japan began to occupy the three eastern provinces, we have seen the terms airplanes, bombs, artillery, and tanks, etc., in the newspapers every day, as well as the tragic state of our compatriots in the Northeast losing their country and homes. By January 28th of this year, Japan re-enacted the old trick of the night attack on Shenyang in Shanghai. Therefore, the terms that we only saw in the newspapers before, we now see with our own eyes and hear with our own ears. The tragic state of our compatriots in distress that we only saw in the newspapers before, we are now directly or indirectly experiencing. This deep impression is not easy to erase. But we must know that there are two kinds of wars. One is military war, which is what we have experienced since January 28th. The other is commercial war, which we have been experiencing every moment since we were oppressed by imperialism. However, the weapons used in commercial war are not airplanes, artillery, and tanks, so we cannot see the fierce images of bloodshed and flames. Therefore, many people, although they have been experiencing it every day since they were born, do not feel it. The weapon of military war is guns, so we use guns to resist it. The weapon of commercial war is goods, so we use goods to resist it. Speaking of this, I really feel very painful. Since our country has been trading with foreign countries, imports have exceeded exports every year, and this proportion has become larger year by year. The import surplus in the first year of the Republic was more than 21.301 million taels, and by the twentieth year of the Republic, it reached more than 55.985 million taels, an increase of more than two and a half times. Just from the first year of the Republic to the twentieth year, the amount of import surplus in our country has reached more than 39.1223 trillion taels. This is really an alarming number. If we use this money in the country, then there will be great reforms in military affairs, industry, transportation, internal affairs, education, and society. Our country will not be so poor and weak now. But the money has flowed to foreign countries, so our country's rural areas are bankrupt, industry is declining, and commerce is on the verge of death, living completely under the breath of imperialism. Now, our country's national economy has reached the point of bankruptcy. Are we going to sit and wait for death? Don't we want to get up and find a way to resist? Last time, when our 19th Route Army resisted the Japanese invasion of Shanghai, the people of the whole country, especially the people of Shanghai, rose up to help. It can be seen that the people of the whole country are in favor of resistance. This is certainly not just for military invasion, but also for economic invasion. Because no one wants to suffer the loss of their country and home. Since we have determined that we should resist foreign economic invasion, what should we say to resist now? Our country knows that what foreigners use to invade China is goods, so we use goods to resist them. In other words, it is to revitalize domestic goods and replace foreign goods. I really do not believe in that purely idealistic theory, thinking that Chinese people should only use Chinese goods in any situation. Yes, this is certainly 120,000 points should be, but should be one thing, the fact is another thing, human nature, who does not love beautiful, convenient and cheap things, this human desire knows the principles of war, the principles can not be maintained for long, we have resisted British goods, resisted American goods, Japanese goods, but also resisted many times, but can not last, just take this deeply painful experience to resist Japanese goods, now the newspapers have daily news of large amounts of Japanese goods imported, in North China, and obviously selling Japanese goods, some people have criticized Chinese only five minutes of heat, which is human nature, any kind of nation, in this situation, can not avoid this phenomenon, if we recognize this point, then we can fundamentally seek remedy, otherwise, just talking on paper, the result is still following the previous failure, the fundamental reason is what, is to improve domestic goods, we have to put the advantages of foreign goods, are in domestic goods, and try to increase production in order to popularize, above I have said that people's common psychology, on the one hand for foreign economic Zhenru Market Opened Yesterday 115

Baowei Tuan (Militia) Members Arrested Were Released on Bail Last Night

The merchants and residents of Zhenru, angered by the Municipal Public Security Bureau's arrest of Wang Shouyu, head of the Baowei Tuan, and others, due to a kidnapping case, went on strike the day before yesterday afternoon. Yesterday, municipal commissioners petitioned the municipal government and other agencies, securing their immediate release on bail. The merchants and residents accepted the advice to resume business first. Details of the situation are as follows:

Traitor Missing: During the Japanese occupation of Zhenru, the Japanese appointed the traitor Shen Songge as the chairman of the Zhenru Local Maintenance Association, acting as a puppet and mistreating the citizens in every possible way. On May 23rd, at 11:00 AM, after the Japanese troops withdrew, our forces took over at 2:00 PM that afternoon. Around 1:00 PM, the citizens, filled with hatred, detained the traitor at Yangjia Bridge in Zhenru and then released him. At that time, the Public Security Bureau and the Baowei Tuan were busy restoring order and could not attend to this matter. Later, his wife, Shen Mu (also known as Mu Guiying), reported to the Municipal Public Security Bureau that her husband, Shen Songge, was missing and his whereabouts unknown, accusing Wang Shouyu, head of the local Baowei Tuan, Zhou Xilian, the first squad leader, Gu Jinbao, the second squad leader, Xu Peinan, the independent squad platoon leader, and members Huang Chungeng, Gan Yuhong, Cai Qirong, Pan Jinkui, Zhao Xianshan, squad member Fu Zhongmin, clerk Yang Asi, and Li Xiaoshi, the firefighting director of the fire brigade, of kidnapping.

Arrest with Evidence: After receiving the report, the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Wen Yingxing, considering the case involved kidnapping, assigned it to the Detective Squad. The squad leader, Lu Ying, ordered detectives to take Shen Mu's servant, surnamed Yang, as a witness and drove to Zhenru to make arrests on the morning before yesterday at 7:00 AM. They first went to the Baowei Tuan headquarters at Xianghua Bridge. As Wang Shouyu and the squad leaders were out, they arrested Huang Chunxiang, the owner of Yichangxiang Foreign Goods Store and member of the Baowei Tuan, and Fu Zhongmin. They then went to the residence of the head of the Baowei Tuan at Xigang Dam, took a photo of Wang Shouyu, and questioned his nephew, Wang Zhixian. Next, they went to the residence of Zhou Xilian on Beida Street and arrested his brother, Zhou Xiwangsheng, before releasing him on bail. They also went to the residence of Xu Peinan, the independent squad platoon leader at Yuji Water Plant on Jiaotong Road, but failed to apprehend him. They then returned to the bureau to report.

Town-Wide Strike: All 242 stores in Zhenru, including Zhang He Tai, Ding Tai, Yixin Sauce Garden, Shengji Renhao, Wang Changhe, Zhang Deyuan, Ding Xin Tai, Tai He, Zhi Xiang, Gan Caishan Tang, Sheng Chang Xiang, Yi Chang Xiang, Qia Xing, He Xing, Bao Xie Ji, Yan Yuan Feng, and Pu Cheng Ji, believed that Wang Shouyu and the other eleven members of the Baowei Tuan were all reputable merchants. During the recent war of resistance against Japan, they made significant contributions to the rear supply of the army, and their merits were widely acknowledged. Outraged by the traitor's false accusations, they collectively went on strike at 2:00 PM in the afternoon to support them and sent representatives to plead with Wang Binchan, the head of the Shanghai North Baowei Tuan, and others to find ways to rescue them.

Rescues from All Sides: Wang Binchan, the head of the Shanghai North Baowei Tuan, Hong Lanxiang, the municipal commissioner of Zhenru, and Yang Fuyuan, the head of the Caohejing Baowei Tuan, went to the Municipal Government to see Mayor Wu Tiecheng yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, as the day before yesterday was a Sunday and government offices were closed, requesting him to send someone to investigate thoroughly and bring the truth to light. The Secretary-General, Yu Hongjun, received them and promised to instruct the Public Security Bureau to investigate. The original petition is recorded as follows: A petition for reporting matters. Wang Shouyu, head of the Baowei Tuan in our district, and eleven other squad leaders including Tong Xilian were falsely accused of being kidnapping bandits. Yesterday morning at 8:00 AM, members of the Detective Squad of the Public Security Bureau came to Zhenru to arrest them. As Wang Tuanzheng and Zhou DuiZhang were out on official duty, the squad members went to Wang’s house to search, took a photo of Wang, and took away Huang Chungeng and Fu Zhongmin, two members of our town’s Baowei Tuan. The merchants and residents of our town believe that Wang and others are enthusiastic about local public welfare, protect the township, and have made great contributions. Now they are groundlessly accused, which causes great panic. We request that the two arrested people be released first, and that the accusers be punished in return. Wang is also a municipal commissioner of this town, with a substantial family fortune and careful in his work. I have worked with him for many years, and I immediately sent someone to comfort him. I specially report to you, please send someone to investigate thoroughly and check whether there is any suspicion of framing, so that the truth can come to light.

Page 10

I await your orders with urgency.

Persuading to Reopen the Market: At 8:00 AM yesterday morning, the Municipal Public Security Bureau sent Deputy Inspector-General Jiang Baixiang to Zhenru to persuade the stores to reopen. He, along with the director of the West District Third Sub-Bureau and business representatives Xu Yizhou and Yang Yiqing, persuaded them to reopen the market first. Huang Chungeng and Fu Zhongmin, the arrested members of the Baowei Tuan, were allowed to be released on bail and to be summoned at any time. However, this would have to be decided after consulting Director Wen in the afternoon. After repeated persuasion by Deputy Inspector-General Jiang, all the stores temporarily reopened for business at 10:00 AM yesterday morning. However, if they still could not be released on bail in the afternoon, they decided to go on strike again the next day.

Efforts to Secure Bail: Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Zhenru Municipal Commissioner Hong Lanxiang and business representatives Yang Diankui and others went to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to secure bail. They prepared letters of guarantee from the Municipal Committee and the Baowei Tuan headquarters, as well as documents from thirty stores including Zhang He Tai and Yang Wanshun, jointly certifying Wang Shouyu and the other eleven members of the Baowei Tuan. Wu Zhiquan, the chief of the Third Section, received them. The letter of certification is recorded as follows: Director, greetings. We, the people of our district, are indignant about the case in which Wang Shouyu, head of our district’s Baowei Tuan, was falsely accused by Shen Songge, the chairman of the Maintenance Association under the Japanese occupation. Wang has always been fair and selfless. During this war of resistance against Japan, he made great contributions to the rear supply of the Nineteenth Route Army, and his merits are widely acknowledged. We all deeply admire and support him. Moreover, Wang has a substantial family fortune and would never engage in illegal activities. We hereby jointly certify that Wang is a loyal and dedicated person, and we take full responsibility. We ask you to investigate and acknowledge our public sentiment. We respectfully offer this letter and wish you good health.

Welcoming Release from Prison: Wu Zhiquan, chief of the Third Section of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, allowed Huang Chungeng and Fu Zhongmin to be released on bail without interrogation, as they had just been brought in from the Inspectorate. He scheduled a hearing for 2:00 PM this afternoon to determine the truth. Commissioner Hong then transported Huang and Fu back to Zhenru by car. All the citizens, having heard the news in advance, waited at the back gate and other places to welcome them warmly. The stores set off firecrackers. Huang and Fu expressed their gratitude to those who welcomed them and returned to the Tuan headquarters to resume their duties.

District Meetings: The Municipal Baowei Tuan Reorganization Committee sent Adjutant Yu Yuanjue to investigate yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. Furthermore, the Baowei Tuan headquarters of Wusong, Pengpu, Caojing, and other districts, in order to protect the service personnel of the Baowei Tuan, have reportedly scheduled a meeting to discuss solutions.

Various Industries

Deliberating on the Reconstruction of the Disaster Area 116

Decided to Establish a Trade and Industry Rehabilitation Association

Petitioning the Government to Exempt the Disaster Area from National Taxes

Merchants from various industries in the disaster-stricken areas of this city, in order to seek the revival of industry and commerce, gathered at Yipinxiang Western Restaurant at 7:00 PM the night before last to discuss the process. They decided to organize a Disaster Area Trade and Industry Rehabilitation Association, and to petition the National Government to exempt the disaster area from national taxes, and issued a declaration. Details of the situation are as follows:

Attending Representatives: Qiu Liangyu and Cao Zhaoguang of the Shanghai North Road Merchants General Federation, Li Ruzhang of the Paint and Woodware Industry Association, Zhou Shiheng of the Bookstore Industry Association, Zhang Dalian of the Sauce and Liquor Industry Association, Luo Shouxian of the Ice Factory Industry Association, Cheng Guichu of the Face Powder Industry Association, Gu Yixiang of the Cotton Ginning Industry Association, Hu Yuantang of the Restaurant Industry Association, Che Lisheng of the Rickshaw Industry Association, Jin Guifu of the Fresh Meat Industry Association, Lu Zhankui of the Umbrella Industry Association, Pan Xusheng of the Mercerized Cotton Weaving Industry Association, Xiao Zheming of the Pawnshop Industry Association, Xie Zhongle of the Flying Flower Association, Zhong Yibo of the Jiangwan Branch of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Yuzhi of the Wusong Branch of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and over a hundred others.

Chairman's Report: Ye Jiaxing, elected as chairman, reported, "I have invited everyone here today because you are all leaders of various industries in the disaster area. Since the January 28th Incident, when the Japanese army invaded Shanghai, Wusong, Jiangwan, Zhabei, and other places have been turned into scorched earth. The once prosperous and thriving commercial districts have been reduced to ashes. The estimated losses are over 160 million yuan, which is truly appalling. Now that the war has ceased, these areas have been successively taken over. The most important thing now is to handle the aftermath and revive industry and commerce. The Municipal Government of this city has already organized a Disaster Area Relief Committee to be responsible for handling the aftermath, which shows that the government also has a strong desire to revive the destroyed industry and commerce. However, for the revival of industry and commerce in the disaster area, merchants who have personally experienced the pain should rise up to rescue and revive their own industry and commerce. It is essential to unify our steps. First, we should ask the government authorities to find ways to provide relief. Second, we should find ways to revive the disaster area that has been turned into ruins. For example, those who have borrowed money from banks and money houses are now heavily indebted and cannot continue to do business. All of these should be provided with relief so that their debts can be gradually repaid and they do not fall into a state of stagnation. We need to invite experienced and reputable people to assist us. Today, I ask everyone to express their opinions and work together to achieve the goal of revival."

Important Resolutions: (1) Resolved to establish the Shanghai Disaster Area Industry and Commerce Rehabilitation Committee; (2) Resolved that the committee should consist of 21 members, and nominated Ye Jiaxing, Zhang Yuzhi, Jin Guifu, Zhong Yibo, Wu Zhonggao, Zhang Dalian, Luo Shouxian, Jin Wenxiang, Xiao Zheming, Qiu Liangyu, Zhou Shiheng, Gu Yuantang, Xie Zhongle, Xia Xiaofang, Pan Xusheng, Chen Songyuan, Cheng Guichu, Li Ruzhang, Yuan Hongjun, Zhu Yiqian, and Cai Qiajun as members; (3) Resolved that Ye Jiaxing should be the convener of the first executive committee meeting; (4) Resolved to petition the National Government to issue relief bonds for reconstruction; (5) Resolved to petition the National Government to exempt the disaster area from national taxes until it recovers to the pre-war state; (6) Resolved to petition the Municipal Government to exempt the disaster area from all local taxes until it recovers to the pre-war state; (7) Resolved that the association should issue a declaration, and nominated Yuan Hongjun, Zhou Shiheng, and Sun Mingqi to draft it.

Japanese Military Activities

Causing Misunderstandings Among Residents 117

Japanese Navy Frequently Fires Guns for Demonstration

Residents Start Moving Out in Alarm

Around 8:45 AM yesterday morning, about 50 to 60 fully armed Japanese naval marines in four military vehicles turned from Jiaotong Road onto Zhongshan Road and drove east. It was reported that these Japanese soldiers were from the Toyota Cotton Mill. Also, at 11:50 AM, a vehicle with about 20 armed Japanese naval marines drove westward on Zhongxing Road in Zhabei. Recently, the Japanese navy stationed here often fired guns in demonstration at night. Two gunshots were heard near Zhongxing Bridge the night before last, causing rumors to spread in the Zhabei area. Yesterday afternoon, it was widely rumored that there was a conflict between Japanese troops and the police. Residents became alarmed and even started moving out. In fact, all of these were unfounded and mere rumors.

Wu Tiecheng Inspects War Zone Yesterday 118

Asked About the Hardships of Disaster Victims, Offering Comfort

Mayor Wu Tiecheng, along with Northeast representative Zhang Xueming, and takeover committee members Yin Rugeng, Li Mo, Li Shengjun, Public Security Bureau members Gong XiKui, Huang Ming, Yin Tixin, etc., departed for the war zone for inspection at 8:30 AM yesterday. A police motorcycle team from the Public Security Bureau led the way for security. They first went to the Wusong Fort, where Li Jing, the Seventh District Chief, accompanied and guided them. After inspecting the north and south forts in detail, they saw that all the fort positions had been completely destroyed, and they could not help but sigh with regret. Then they went to Wusong Town, Yinxiang Port, Hongzhen, etc. for inspection. They briefly rested at the Third Sub-Bureau of the Fifth District and had lunch. In the afternoon, they went to Jiangwan Town for inspection. The houses in Jiangwan that were destroyed in the war have now been rebuilt. Mayor Wu immediately told them that the roads should be widened, etc. After inspecting Jiangwan in detail, they went to Zhabei for inspection. First, they went to the Zhabei Office of the Public Security Bureau, and then to the Fifth District Office of the Public Security Bureau. Mayor Wu gave detailed instructions on maintaining public order. Afterward, they patrolled the surrounding area of Zhabei and returned to the Municipal Government at about 3:00 PM. During the inspection, Mayor Wu inquired in detail about the local disaster-stricken compatriots to understand the true hardships and realities, providing a reference for disaster relief.

Visiting the Destroyed Dragon King Temple 119

The Dragon King Temple in the Sanjiashui area outside of Wusong is a must-pass for foreign ships coming to Shanghai. In 1927, due to the attack on the Wusong Fort by the Haiqi ship of the Northeast Fleet, the military and political authorities set up two cannons there and stationed more than 40 artillerymen. This time, it was destroyed by a Japanese warship. The reporter and a friend passed by the area the day before yesterday. As the destroyed cannons had not yet been removed, the reporter recorded the situation as follows: The cannon was manufactured by the Jiangnan Cannon Factory in the year of Guimao in the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty. The cannon was about 1.5 zhang long and had a caliber of 4.6 chi. It was destroyed at 3:00 PM on February 3 this year. The two cannons lay horizontally on the seawall, with the cannon mouths facing south. One cannon was hit by a Japanese warship in the middle and was broken into two sections, causing the front section to be thrown more than 2 zhang into the field. The rear of one cannon was hit, causing the tail to be destroyed. The cannon base was built of cement, in the shape of a millstone, and was destroyed by Japanese aircraft.

Wang Xiaolai's Letter to Various Trade Associations

Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, sent letters to various trade associations yesterday, stating: "The outbreak of the Shanghai Incident shocked the world. This is why the Bereaved Families of Fallen Soldiers Fostering Association was established in a timely manner. However, the association has been established for almost two months, and the measures for fostering the bereaved families need to be implemented urgently. Raising funds is particularly urgent. I have long admired your association's concern for the national crisis and its deep sympathy. The work of the association needs your attention. I have attached the donation register and ask you to check and receive it. Please encourage donations, and send the collected funds to the receiving bank or money house.

Distributing Relief Rice to Impoverished Households in Jiangwan Regularly 122

In order to provide relief to disaster victims, the Jiangwan District Disaster-Stricken Compatriots United Association sent personnel to the countryside to investigate impoverished households and use it as a standard for providing relief. They also stipulated a review standard based on five items: houses, property, population, fields, and pre-disaster living conditions, dividing them into three levels, A, B, and C, in percentage terms. 408 households (extremely poor) were approved for level A, with 735 adults and 522 children; 263 households (less poor) were approved for level B, with 674 adults and 236 children. The Relief Committee of the Association has decided to distribute 100 bags of relief rice from the Catholic Church in Hongkou first, stipulating 6 sheng for adults and 4 sheng for children in extremely poor households, and 5 sheng for adults and 3 sheng for children in less poor households. The distribution date is from June 7 to 10. After the distribution is completed, the Lianyi Xiang Association will continue to distribute relief according to the register of impoverished households investigated by the Association. It is reported that after these two distributions, the living conditions of the households in the A category can be barely maintained. In addition to appropriating 250 bags of rice for the relief of the A and B categories, the remaining will be used for the relief of the C category households.

The Flood Relief Association Allocates Relief Funds Discretionarily 123

Continued Loan of American Wheat Did Not Materialize

Zhu Ziqiao, Director of the Work Group of the National Government Flood Relief Committee, stated that although the committee had purchased 450,000 tons of American wheat and distributed more than 7 million yuan in relief funds and cotton clothing, the disaster area was too large and there were too many disaster victims, so it was insufficient to provide relief. At this time of scarcity, although Chairman Song intended to continue to borrow 100,000 tons of American wheat to help the disaster victims, as soon as this proposal was made, requests for allocation from various disaster areas came one after another. Due to the difficulty of raising funds in China and the recent situation of American finance, the issue of continuing to borrow American wheat ultimately became a pie in the sky. Director Zhu still believes that in the areas with the most severe disasters, there are indeed disaster victims who cannot survive without relief. He made every effort to scrape together funds and allocated them at his discretion to the provinces with the most severe disasters, such as Jiangsu, Anhui, and Hubei, to eliminate the tragedy of starving people in the wilderness.

Christians Eagerly Participate in Disaster Relief 125

The China National Christian Council at No. 23 Yuanmingyuan Road in this city, in addition to handling national church cooperation affairs, also cares about social service undertakings. In the past, during the drought in the Northwest, the council collected more than 2 million yuan in donations from churches across the country and asked voluntary experts to handle emergency relief and work relief, such as dredging rivers and building embankments. Disaster victims benefited greatly. Last year, during the floods in various ports along the Yangtze River, churches across the country once again competed to be the first to donate. As of the end of May this year, in addition to donating more than 200,000 yuan to American churches through specialized committees for relief, it directly received more than 156,000 yuan in donations. The funds were allocated for emergency relief in Anhui, Hubei, Jiangsu, Jiangxi, and Hunan provinces through local church groups, and work-for-relief programs were implemented. Agricultural relief loans were also launched in these provinces, with Chinese and Western experts responsible for investigation and guidance, so that farmers could obtain loans to purchase agricultural tools and seeds for cultivation. Also, when the Japanese soldiers attacked Shanghai, during the two or three months, churches from various places sent money to the council, asking for relief for wounded soldiers and refugees. As of now, a total of about 12,000 yuan has been used for refugees and about 6,000 yuan has been used for wounded soldiers. More than 1,000 yuan was directly sent to the Nineteenth Route Army to provide relief to wounded soldiers. It is reported that the expenses of the council for handling various disaster relief work, such as staff salaries, stationery, and other expenses, have never been deducted from the relief funds. Even the salaries of the personnel who personally went to the disaster area to handle relief work were paid separately by the local church groups. All donations can be used for disaster relief, so the council has won the trust of churches at home and abroad.

Bureau of Weights and Measures

Yesterday Begins Inspection of New Instruments 132

Since its establishment last year under orders, the Municipal Bureau of Weights and Measures has been rectifying old weights and measures and replacing them with new ones in stages. Although the time has been short, the results have been remarkable. Subsequently, due to the Shanghai Incident, the work was suspended. The bureau feared that citizens might become accustomed to using old instruments again. Therefore, starting yesterday, they dispatched many male and female staff members, along with patrol officers from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, to various vegetable markets in the Nanshi (Southern City) to conduct inspections. If any old instruments are found to be in use, they will be destroyed on the spot, and the users will be ordered to purchase new instruments. It is reported that the inspection of the Zhabei (Northern Shanghai) commercial district will continue next week.

This Year's Second Cholera Report 133

Ten Deaths Last Week

Wu Liande of the Harbor Quarantine Office, yesterday released this year's second cholera report, which is recorded as follows: (1) Last week (ending June 4th), there were 92 cholera cases in this city (including 10 deaths). The numbers are presented in the table below:

District Number of Cases Number of Deaths

Shanghai City 55 6

International Settlement 27 3

French Concession 10 1

Total 92 10

The number of cases this week, combined with the previously reported total, is 190 cases. (2) The new patients discovered last week are scattered in various hospitals. Their numbers are listed as follows:

Shanghai Epidemic Hospital 70

Emergency Epidemic Hospital 11

Haig Road Refugee Hospital 1

Shanghai Public Hospital 2

Shanghai Municipal Council Isolation Hospital 8

(3) Shanghai hospitals have long been preparing more than a thousand beds to accommodate patients. The Shanghai Municipal Council Isolation Hospital can accommodate 200 people, the Shanghai Epidemic Hospital on Xizang Road can accommodate 150 people, the Emergency Epidemic Hospital can accommodate 200 people, the Red Cross Epidemic Hospital can accommodate 150 people, and the newly established Infectious Disease Hospital at the French Concession's Guangci Hospital can accommodate 30 people. It is hoped that the health authorities of all sectors can accommodate cholera patients as much as possible when necessary. (4) Four notable cases of cholera patients are briefly described below: A. Ito Hidejiro, a Japanese national, 35 years old, residing on North Sichuan Road, contracted the disease on May 26th and was sent to the Shanghai Municipal Council Isolation Hospital on May 29th. Bacteriological examination confirmed cholera, and he died the next day. B. A Japanese patient named Miki, 34 years old, came to Shanghai from Osaka and stayed for several days. He contracted the disease on May 31st and returned to his country on the Shanghai Maru mail ship. On June 3rd, he arrived in Kobe, where the local health authorities confirmed through bacteriological examination that he had genuine cholera. C. Sailor Wu Da, 42 years old, arrived in Shanghai from Australia on the Sydneyia ship on May 18th. On May 28th, he was sent

to Renji Hospital and then transferred to the Shanghai Municipal Council Isolation Hospital the next day. Cholera was confirmed, and he died on June 2nd. At that time, the ship was inspected by the Harbor Quarantine Office and strictly disinfected and fumigated before departing for Japan on June 4th. D. A Russian patient named Sunuvich, 42 years old, came to Shanghai from Tianjin. He contracted the disease on May 27th and was sent to the Shanghai Municipal Council Isolation Hospital, where he died on the 30th. (5) The Red Cross Epidemic Hospital, located opposite the Racecourse near the New World, will open on June 9th, and we will have another 150 beds to accommodate patients. (6) Within the past week, Nanjing reported 5 cases of cholera, and Hankou reported 20 cases, including one death. (7) On May 14th, the Dutch East Indies declared Shanghai a cholera-infected port, followed by Singapore on May 21st. (8) Recently, there has been much discussion attributing the cause of cholera transmission to the dumping of sewage into the Huangpu River. According to scientific theory (this should not be considered the main cause of transmission; in other words, sewage itself cannot cause cholera, and the transmission is actually caused by the excretion of cholera patients or carriers). An examination of the water source of the Shanghai Waterworks Company shows that the water is taken from the best part of the Huangpu River. It would be better to improve it slightly, especially before filtration. However, the majority of Shanghai's poor have no way to obtain pure drinking water. The more residents in this harsh environment, the more unmanageable the situation becomes. From this perspective, Shanghai's health authorities and other charitable organizations must urgently seek remedial measures to eradicate this epidemic. (9) There has been progress in vaccination work. The number of injections administered is as follows:

District April May

Shanghai City None 97,117

International Settlement None 27,855

French Concession 4,125 9,118

Total 4,125 134,190

Page 11

Local News II

Tenants on Dongmen Road Write to Discuss Rent Calculation Methods 139

Rent Calculated at 8% of Land Value and Construction Cost

Since the reconstruction of Dongmen Road from the merging of Jishui and Fangbang Roads in Nanshi, the rent for the houses has increased several times. Recently, after the January 28th Shanghai Incident, businesses have suspended operations to resist the enemy. Although peace has been declared and the market is recovering, the losses of the businesses have been enormous, and the exorbitant rent makes it difficult to maintain operations. The Dongmen Road Business Community Tenants' Association has been formed and sent letters to the landlords yesterday, stating, "To Whom It May Concern: In order to revitalize the municipal administration and enhance prosperity, the local authorities merged Jishui and Fangbang Roads and reconstructed them into Dongmen Road. The people of Shanghai consider its situation superior and its location important, giving it the beautiful name of 'Model Road.' However, its commerce has become inversely proportional, and it has not seen much improvement compared to the former Jishui and Fangbang Roads. Since the Shanghai Incident, it has become even more deserted, and several businesses are even considering closing down. More than a dozen new houses are empty. We are alarmed by this situation. Upon investigation, the amount of rent has increased several times or even dozens of times compared to before, which is far from the current business situation. Whether in ancient or modern times, at home or abroad, the level of housing rent has always depended on the prosperity of the land, industry, and commerce. There has never been a case where industry and commerce are not developed, but the rent can be increased alone. If this principle is reversed, industry and commerce cannot prosper, and how can municipal administration develop? It is tantamount to driving oneself to suicide. Moreover, the houses on this road are mostly small and cramped, only suitable for small and medium-sized businesses. The huge rent is beyond their financial capacity. Therefore, the houses on this road that have not been rented out are not inquired about, and those that have been rented out are in a situation where they cannot maintain their operations. The deserted market shows the reason for this. On the landlords' side, although there is a huge rent income, the obstruction of municipal development and the vacancy of houses result in losses that outweigh the gains. For the sake of the future of the municipal administration, the prosperity of this road, the interests of the landlords, and our own operations, we have jointly formed this association to achieve a consistent goal through legal procedures. Since rent is closely related to municipal administration and commerce, its increase or decrease must conform to the times, adapt to the environment, and consider the economic strength of the citizens to deliberate and revise it. The houses that have been built for several years and have not been rented out, the landlords have now realized and voluntarily reduced or exempted the rent. The fairest method is to follow the regulations of the municipal government from the previous year and calculate the rent at 8% of the combined value of the land and construction cost. We are based on this standard, and we have prepared a table estimating the rental value of this road, and we have generously included depreciation over ten years, and all insurance and repair costs are added in. We hereby send this letter representing the consensus of the tenants on this road, along with the table (omitted). We hope that you will consider and respond accordingly."

Yan Yutang Escapes Danger 142

The New World Gains a Suspect

A Large Number of Military Supplies Seized from the Bandit's Den

Yesterday the Main Perpetrator of the Kidnapping was Investigated

All Auditions are Strictly Prohibited

Yan Yutang, the owner of the Dalong Iron Factory and the Suzhou Lensa Factory at the end of Xiaoshadu Road, lives at No. 1 Pingliang Road in East Shanghai. In addition to the above two factories, Yan also runs a real estate business and founded Guangyu Business Company at No. 58 Guangdong Road and Jiangxi Road. On the morning of the 4th of last month, at 8:45, Yan took his own car No. 8967 to Guangyu Company to work. Just as he arrived at the entrance of the company, he was suddenly kidnapped by several bandits who demanded a ransom of 500,000 yuan. Yan's family reported to the police and requested an investigation. More than a month has passed, and there has been no news. Until about 11:30 the night before yesterday, Lu Liankui, the Chinese Chief Inspector of the General Patrol Department, received a tip-off that several bandits involved in the case were hiding in Room 337 of the New World Hotel on Xizang Road. Inspector Lu immediately dispatched Chinese Inspector Liu Shaokui, Detectives Feng Zhiming, Wang Chengying, Zhou Honglin, Wu Changkai, Yin Zhanqing, Shen Tianbao, and others to the hotel. They opened another room, No. 336, opposite Room 337, to monitor the actions of the occupants of the room. After investigation, it was found that the people in the room were highly suspected of being involved in the Yan case. Therefore, Wang Jian from Zhenjiang, Kong Ali from Ningbo, Chen Huixing from Jiangbei, Dong Xiaosi, and Ye Xianglian from Pudong, five people in total, were arrested and taken to the police station. Under questioning, Liang was identified as the main perpetrator of the Yan kidnapping. Wang Jian also confessed that the hostage was hidden at No. 72 Baier Shao Road and Pushi Road in the French Concession. Inspector Lu and others immediately cooperated with Chinese and foreign detectives from the French Concession Police to rescue him. However, the bandits guarding the hostage had already fled after hearing the news. Yan Yutang was found locked in the room. The detectives immediately rescued Yan and seized three Mauser pistols, 163 bullets, one handgun, 31 bullets, one gas pistol (pen-style), and two bottles of narcotics in the house, and brought them all to the police station. Yesterday morning, Wang and others were escorted to the First Special District Court, Criminal Division 1, where Judge Qian Hongye presided over the trial. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, requested the court to prohibit audience during the interrogation, because the case was serious and the main criminals had not been arrested. He feared that Wang and others might reveal the main criminals during the interrogation and leak secrets. Judge Qian granted the request, so the details of the interrogation could not be recorded. It was found that Yan Yutang had been kidnapped unsuccessfully in September 1928. Yan's chauffeur, Mr. Jia, was shot and wounded by bandits. This was the second time he had been kidnapped.

Ma Er, a Murderer and Robber

Ma Er Executed by Firing Squad 143

Ma Asks to Notify His Father to Collect the Body

Obscene and Disrespectful Language to Detective Cai

Ma Er, 28 years old, from Tongzhou, nicknamed "Little Yellow Hair," was a chauffeur for Chinese Detective Cai Zhitian at the Huishan Police Station. On the midnight of September 18th last year, he and his accomplices broke into the home of Zhu Liangshan from Qingpu at No. 196 Dongxi Huade Road, killed Zhu's relative, Madam Gu Tan, and the maid, Zhou Luo, and stole property worth 1,038 yuan. The case was solved and the perpetrators were arrested by Detective Cai, and Ma Er was sent to the First Special District Court where he confessed clearly and was sentenced to death. After the approval of his superiors, yesterday morning was the date of execution. The police escorted Ma to the Third Court, where the executing Judge Fu presided over the session. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, ordered the police to present Ma Er to the court. The judge asked him if he had any last words and if he wanted to send a letter to his family. Ma said that his father's name was Ma Hongkun, and he lived at No. 1312 Longqing Lane, Ti Lan Qiao. He asked to be notified to collect the body. He also used obscene and disrespectful language towards Detective Cai. Judge Fu then ordered him to be sent to the Shanghai Local Court Procuratorate for execution according to law. The Chinese and foreign police officers escorted Ma, along with the case files and photos, in a car to the Caohejing execution ground. The prosecutor appointed by the local court arrived at the scene, verified Ma's identity, and ordered the judicial police to bind him and execute him by firing squad according to law.

Extortionists in a Hurry 144

Arrested Near the Train Station

A Tailor is Suspected of Writing the Letter

Chen Yushun, the manager of Yuantaiheng Seafood Store at No. 15 Yanghang Street in the French Concession, previously received a threatening letter signed "Li," demanding 10,000 yuan and arranging a meeting at the Nanyang Hotel in Xiaodongmen on the 3rd of this month. At that time, Chen sent Xu Jingfu as his representative to meet the extortionists, He Yongli and Zhou A'ming from Ningbo, but the negotiations failed. The meeting was rescheduled for that evening at the Nanyang Hotel on North Zhejiang Road. Chen again sent his cousin, Jiang Lianfu, to the meeting. Upon arrival, Jiang found only one extortionist, He, in the room, and he suddenly became bold. He turned around and went outside, called the police, and had He arrested and sent to the First Special District Court for investigation, etc. It has been reported in this newspaper. It is now learned that Zhou was originally with He that evening, but Zhou was acting as a lookout outside the hotel. When He was arrested, Zhou immediately fled, and thus escaped. The next day, at 2:30 PM, Zhou led his wife and a girl to the North Train Station, intending to flee to another port. His hurried appearance was noticed by a detective stationed on the street, who immediately arrested him and took him to the Huisi Police Station. Under interrogation, he fully confessed and revealed that the person who wrote the threatening letter was hiding at No. 265 Tangshan Road. Detective Shang immediately took Zhou to the address and arrested a tailor named Qi Deguang from Liangji. He was taken back to the police station and confronted with He and Zhou. However, Qi insisted that he had never met the two men and had never conspired to send threatening letters. The police chief ordered him to be detained temporarily. Yesterday morning, Zhou and Qi were escorted to the First Special Court, where Judge Feng Shide presided over the trial. First, the police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, recounted the incident and requested that Zhou and others be detained for further investigation, and that a formal indictment be filed together with He, who had been arrested previously, after the investigation was completed. Then, Detective Shang reported the circumstances of the arrest of the two men, and Chen Yushun sent Xu Jingfu to the case to state the circumstances of the negotiations with He and Zhou at the Nanyang Hotel in Xiaodongmen. During the negotiations, the two men said that they needed to borrow 10,000 yuan, otherwise they would do something unfavorable to Chen Yushun. Chen Yushun asked them who the "Li" who signed the letter was, but the two men said that Li was their teacher and was very famous. Chen asked them to introduce them to him, but the two men refused. Since the negotiations were unsuccessful, they rescheduled for later that evening, but Jiang Lianfu went to the negotiations at night, and Chen did not know the details. Zhou A'ming confessed that the threatening letter was written by He. In the afternoon of the 3rd, Zhou went to He's house at No. 624 Xipuyi Lane, Qipu Road. After He went to Xiaodongmen and met with Xu, Zhou learned what He had done. Because the negotiations were unsuccessful, Zhou and He returned home together. He said that since the other party did not agree to give the 10,000 yuan, they should increase the amount, so he wrote another letter demanding 50,000 yuan. He initially ordered Zhou to send it, but because Zhou declined, He personally took the letter alone to Room 3 of the Nanyang Hotel on North Zhejiang Road that evening, intending to ask Jiang Lianfu to pass it on to Chen Yushun. In the afternoon of the 4th, after Zhou was arrested and taken to the police station, He whispered to Zhou during the detective's interrogation, begging Zhou to admit that the letter was written by him, and he would give him 400 yuan. Zhou said that he had a minor grudge against Qi Deguang in the past, so he took the opportunity to falsely accuse Qi of writing the letter, but in fact, Qi had nothing to do with it. Then, Qi was interrogated, and he still swore that he had no association with the gangsters. Judge Feng then ordered Zhou and Qi to be remanded in custody for further trial together with He Yongli.

French Concession

Strict Suppression of Prostitution 145

Pimps and Brothel Owners to Hold a Regular General Meeting

To Discuss Countermeasures

Since the arrival of Commissioner of Police Fébvre in the French Concession a few months ago, in addition to strictly prohibiting opium and gambling, he has also actively suppressed various prohibited activities such as prostitutes and streetwalkers forcibly soliciting customers. Every day, he dispatches a large number of Chinese and Annamese police, traveling in patrol cars to arrest people everywhere. At night, plainclothes detectives are sent out, disguised as coolies, to continue the arrests, with fines and other punishments imposed. Therefore, those engaged in the profession are all worried, not knowing whether to laugh or cry. In the past, when the lanterns were first lit, groups of women in pink and green lined the streets, but now they have completely disappeared, creating a desolate scene unprecedented in the history of the concession. Brothel owners and meat market bosses, seeing that the business has declined sharply recently, and fearing that it will be difficult to maintain the status quo if this continues, are said to be planning to convene a general meeting of all pimps and brothel owners before the 10th of this month.

To consider countermeasures. It is noted that there was previously an organization called the "Pingkang Guild" in the French Concession, with the chairman being a famous brothel owner named Wu, which was quite large in scale, like a legal institution. However, Wu enriched himself during his tenure and was soon reported, so Wu fled, and the large-scale Pingkang Guild also disappeared as a result. As for this general meeting of pimps and brothel owners, it is said that they will expand the organization and try their best to save the critical situation.

Verdict in the Security Gun Tax Company Case 146

Shen Changlin and Others Sentenced Separately

Previously, someone illegally established a "Security Gun Tax Company" at No. 8 Bulinli, Avenue Edward VII, specializing in protecting illegal opium dens and collecting gun taxes daily. As soon as preparations and registration began, the French police detective discovered the company's fraudulent fundraising scheme. He immediately dispatched detectives to arrest seventeen staff members, including Zhang Shengfu, and confiscated signboards, books, registration certificates, stationery, and other items. They were sent to the Second Special District Court, and the police prosecuted them for the crime of jointly defrauding money under Article 363 of the Criminal Law. After Judge Zhang Chaozuo held two hearings and thoroughly investigated, the defendants, defended by lawyers Jin Yu and Wang Shizong, etc., were declared to have completed the trial and set a date for sentencing. Except for Zhang Shengfu and Wang Guihua, who were released on bail, the others were returned to custody to await instructions, as previously reported. The presiding judge has now carefully reviewed the confessions of the defendants and, based on the severity of the circumstances, has prepared a judgment. Yesterday was the date for sentencing. The bailed defendants, each accompanied by their representative lawyer, arrived at the court to await instructions. At 10 a.m., Judge Zhang arrived at the First Criminal Court and ordered the defendants to be brought to court. After briefly questioning their ages and occupations, the judgment was pronounced. Shen Changlin, Yu Xueming (i.e., Yu Heming), and Lin Ganzhong were each sentenced to two months of imprisonment for attempted fraud, and each fined 400 yuan. Zhang Shengfu, Fang Ziqing, Shi Guifu, and Chen Baorong were each given a reduced sentence of one month of imprisonment for assisting in attempted fraud, and each fined 200 yuan. Yu Gansheng, Wang Hengchun, and Wang Guihua were each fined 100 yuan for assisting in attempted fraud. Zhang Debao, Song Bolin, Wang Kailiang, Luo Aquan, Han Huangjin, and Zhou Lansheng were each fined 30 yuan. If they are unable to pay the fines, they will be converted into one day of imprisonment for every two yuan. The number of days of detention before the verdict is finalized will be used to offset the sentence at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment, or one day of detention for two yuan of fine. The copied case books, lead plates, small copper plates, registration certificates, and seals and stationery will be confiscated according to the list. Du Arong is innocent.

Zhou Chunshan Died Happily After Smoking Opium 147

Why Did He Swallow Opium?

The Cause Should Be Investigated

On the 3rd, at around 11 a.m., Zhou Chunshan, a tea merchant from Suzhou, 23 years old, went to the Jiangsu Hotel on Guangdong Road with Xu Xiuying from Shen'an, 26 years old, and booked room 102. The woman went out at around 12 p.m. When she returned to the hotel at around 1 p.m., Zhou ordered a bowl of noodles from the tea boy, Shan Amao. After eating, the two went out together at around 3 p.m. to buy a pair of women's shoes and returned to the hotel at around 5 p.m. At around 8 p.m., the woman saw that Zhou's face was pale, so she called the tea boy and others to send him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he died shortly after. The hospital reported this to the Lao Zha Police Station, and the police sent detectives to investigate. They found a bag of opium under the bed in the room and carried the body to the forensic laboratory on Félan Road. Yesterday morning, Li Ying, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, arrived at the laboratory and confirmed that the body was Zhou Chunshan. According to Xu Xiuying's confession, she met Zhou on the road, and he asked her to go to the hotel with him. Zhou was from Suzhou, and she had known him for more than three years. She knew nothing about him taking poison that day. After obtaining the confession, Mr. Li ruled that the deceased, Zhou Chunshan, was a male who had committed suicide by taking poison during his lifetime. The body was temporarily handed over to the Pushan Cemetery for collection pending collection.

Husband and Wife Quarrel, Leading to Suicide by Hanging 148

Chen Tang Was Unlucky in Marriage

Chen Amao, a 25-year-old electrician from Nantong, married Tang (18 years old) from the same village last winter. They lived at No. 31 Lixing Lane, Jiangyin Street, outside the South Gate. After the marriage, they lived peacefully at first, but recently, Chen lost his job and stayed at home, while Tang worked in a tooth powder factory to maintain their livelihood. The night before, Chen gambled outside, and when he returned home, Tang advised him, and the couple quarreled. Yesterday morning, Tang still went to work at the factory, but returned at around 10 a.m. due to feeling unwell. At around 11 a.m., a female companion visited Chen and Tang's house. She called but received no answer. Suddenly, she discovered Chen Tang had hanged herself in the kitchen. The woman was shocked and screamed loudly. Neighbors gathered and tried to save her, finding her chest still warm, hoping to save her. They tried various methods of rescue, but to no avail. Soon, her body turned cold as ice, and there was no way to bring her back to life. The local police station ordered Tao Xingsheng, the local guard of the 27th Precinct, to report to the local court for an examination. At 5 p.m., Prosecutor Zhao, accompanied by Coroner Shen, arrived at the scene and confirmed that Chen Tang had committed suicide by hanging and that there were no other reasons. They filled out the death certificate and ordered the husband, Chen Amao, to provide a coffin and await instructions.

Appeal from the Workers of the Sanyou Company 149

The Shanghai Seventh District Cotton Textile Industry Union sends a telegram (titles omitted): Looking back to the restoration, the Sanyou Industrial Company used a capital of several hundred yuan to manufacture candle wicks. When the May Fourth Movement occurred, people throughout the country regarded promoting domestic goods as their duty. The Sanyou Industrial Company seized the opportunity to rise and expand in response to the times, recruited capital, organized a limited company, and added the production of triangular brand towels to resist the disappearance of imported goods. Since then, the annual profits have been hundreds of thousands of yuan. The company has flourished and achieved today's success. On the one hand, the company has been good at planning and operation, but on the other hand, it is also due to the hard work of all our workers in production. Since the establishment of our union five years ago, we have not only strictly observed the factory's discipline and never caused any disputes, but also stepped up production and strived for the company's development. The facts are there, and there is no room for denial. However, in 1929, the company recruited additional capital and opened a branch factory in Hangzhou, but regarded the main factory as a burden, getting rid of the old to bring in the new, all with the intention of reducing the wages of the main factory workers. Their malicious intentions are obvious. Since the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the main factory has announced a temporary shutdown, and more than a thousand workers in our union have lost their livelihoods and become displaced and homeless. For four months, we have repeatedly sent representatives to request relief, but the company authorities have repeatedly evaded and refused to accept it. Although the Social Affairs Bureau has repeatedly ordered them to provide relief, the company has refused to comply. When the Japanese troops had just withdrawn, the company dismantled important machinery in the factory and transported it to the Hangzhou branch factory. When the workers noticed this, they had already transported a considerable number of parts. All members of our union, with their livelihoods at stake, tried to stop them, but the company authorities did not repent and ignored the Chinese police's authority. They falsely reported the matter to the police in the concession, acting perversely and disregarding the national system. The police arrested the workers, but since there was no crime to prosecute, they released them. The company, seeing that its plan had failed, published an urgent announcement in the newspaper, stating that the Shanghai main factory had announced a temporary shutdown since the Shanghai Incident, that workers who were unable to add their names had already been given severance pay, that the Japanese troops in the factory had not yet moved out, and that the houses and machinery were in disrepair and could not be started, etc., to cover up the truth from society. Sima Zhao's intentions are well known. All members of our union have served Sanyou for 20 years, but the company authorities do not know how to be grateful and instead recklessly destroy, placing thousands of workers in a desperate situation. The Sanyou Industrial Company, which has always been called upon in society to revitalize industry and reduce unemployment, should not have done this. If the company authorities have sufficient wealth and no intention of operating, they might as well announce it clearly. Why should they vacillate and make excuses? All members of our union are on the verge of starvation. If any unexpected disputes occur, the Sanyou Industrial Company should bear full responsibility. While we still have breath, we vow to fight to the end. We hope that people from all walks of life will give us righteous assistance. Industry is fortunate, society is fortunate. We hereby declare.

Postal Workers' Union: The Postal Workers' Union held its ninth fourth representative assembly yesterday afternoon at 3 p.m., with more than 100 people present. Zhang Kechang, Qi Jiamou, and Cheng Zuoqing were publicly elected as the presidium, Xiao Qingshan as the recorder, and Shi Yinghua as the emcee. First, Chairman Zhang Kechang reported. Important resolutions were passed: (1) To prepare for the new union hall as soon as possible and restore the club. Resolved and passed, to be handled by the executive committee. (2) Members Pan Jiaji, Lu Chunhua, Chen Zude, etc., participated in the union's rescue work and sacrificed themselves for the country. In addition to providing preferential compensation by the union, how should they be commended to highlight their loyalty? Resolved: 1. Hold a memorial service, to be handled by the executive committee. 2. Hang the portraits of the three martyrs in the union hall for permanent commemoration. 3. Purchase a piece of public land in Nanxiang, hold a public burial, and erect a monument to commemorate their loyalty. (3) Member Su Pincai and Chen Fangxiang were killed by Japanese soldiers during the war due to public duty. How should this be expressed? Resolved: 1. Send a letter to the authorities requesting compensation in accordance with the regulations for death due to public duty. 2. Handle the same as items 1 and 2 of the previous case. (4) Commendation of members who worked on the consolidation of the postal base movement. Resolved: 1. The union will issue separate commendations. 2. Request the National Postal Workers' Union to issue separate awards. (5) Executive and supervisory committee members Xing Rongzhao,

Sun Hanliang, Zhao Liancheng, Tan Changde, Yu Zhenting, and members Lu Shijing, Yang Ruilong, Zhang Longhai, Zhang Wanchun, etc., were found to have undermined the consolidation of the postal base movement and violated the union's discipline. How should they be severely punished? Resolved: 1. Announce the crimes of Xing et al. and report to the National Postal Workers' Union for public announcement to postal workers' unions in various places. 2. Remove their positions as executive and supervisory committee members, and the vacancies will be filled by alternates. 3. Permanently expel them from membership. 4. Expel them from the union. 5. Publish a notice to members. (6) At yesterday's meeting, executive committee member Zhu Xuefan, based on confidential reports from various parties, reported to the general meeting on behalf of the executive and supervisory committees the activities and despicable behavior of Xing Rongzhao and others who undermined the consolidation of the postal base movement. He was representing the entire executive and supervisory committees, and at the same time, in accordance with the organization during the strike, was also representing the entire Shanghai Postal Workers' Union. Xing Rongzhao, Zhao Liancheng, Sun Hanliang, and other destroyers deliberately disrupted the meeting and conspired to undermine the union, violating the union's discipline. They published an advertisement in the newspaper warning Zhu Xuefan and others without authorization, which was no different from warning the union. Their intentions were sinister, determined to undermine the union and despise all members, which only exposed their despicable behavior and destructive conspiracy. It should be requested that the general meeting publish a rebuttal to Xing et al.'s advertisement. Resolved: Publish a rebuttal in all newspapers and announce their crimes. (7) Now that treacherous people are surrounding us on all sides and destroyers are thinking of undermining the union for others to use, willingly acting as lackeys, we should strictly prevent it. Resolved: Notify members to prevent it at all times, and general meeting representatives should pay special attention and report union traitors as much as possible. (8) The so-called 30,000 yuan bribery case in the postal protection movement concerns the reputation of the union and all members and should be handed over to the executive and supervisory committees to actively handle legal procedures. Resolved and passed, instructing the executive and supervisory committees to actively handle it.

Gengpian Industry Union: The Shanghai Gengpian Industry Union, after active preparations by Yan Quanrong and others for more than half a year, was interrupted by the January 28th Shanghai Incident. On June 1st, a general meeting of all workers was convened to formally establish the union. The municipal party department and the municipal Social Affairs Bureau approved the dispatch of personnel to guide the meeting. Yan Quanrong and six others were elected as directors on the spot, and Huang Yongcheng and three others were elected as supervisors. They took office and began working immediately and submitted an application for registration to the municipal Social Affairs Bureau.

First District Shipbuilding Industry Union: The Qiuxin Office of the First District Shipbuilding Industry Union of the Shanghai Military Camp held an important meeting yesterday afternoon at 5 p.m. and convened all factory foremen for discussions. Chairman Wang Chengzong discussed and resolved the following matters: (1) Please ask the foremen of each department to be responsible for persuading the members to pay their membership fees as soon as possible. (2) Those who are in arrears for three months will be notified and expelled in accordance with the regulations. (3) Arrears will be paid off by June 30th, otherwise they will be expelled in accordance with the regulations. (4) When the factory adds workers, the foremen must first report to the union so that the union can introduce unemployed members. (5) When the factory's work is slow, workers must be dismissed in the order of last in, first out.
