Wing On Dispensary Shanghai Branch Seeks Land for Reopening 152

The Shanghai branch of Tiger Balm Wing On Dispensary on North Sichuan Road has been established for several years. The owner of the dispensary, Mr. Hu Wenhu, a Chinese overseas in Singapore, was a strong supporter of the Shanghai War, having remitted 20,000 yuan to the Nineteenth Route Army and 10,000 yuan to Madam Liao Zhongkai, He Xiangning, for rescue efforts. The charitable donations collected and remitted by his own Singapore Daily News were also more than 300,000 yuan, which were given to the Nineteenth Route Army, the Shanghai Local Maintenance Committee, and the wounded soldiers' hospital run by Soong Ching-ling. The branch in Shanghai was forced to temporarily close due to the impact of the war. Now that the Shanghai war has ended, Mr. Hu believes that the branch should reopen as soon as possible. He has specially dispatched Mr. Hu Guigeng to Shanghai to serve as the general manager of the branch and plan the reopening. The former manager, Mr. Li, has also returned to Shanghai with Mr. Hu. It is said that Mr. Li will return to the Singapore headquarters after completing the handover at the branch. Mr. Hu Guigeng has always had a good reputation in the Chinese overseas community in Singapore and has also worked hard for social welfare and education. He also has a history in the newspaper industry, having served as the president of the Yangon Burma Morning Post, the president of the Singapore Star News, and was also one of the founders of the Singapore Daily News.

Thieves Posing as Postmen Delivering Letters 153

The Owner Opened the Door and Realized He Had Been Tricked

Three Thieves Arrested and Sentenced to Imprisonment

At a certain family home at No. 3 Xiaoshadu Road, West Shanghai, at midnight on the 27th of last month, someone suddenly knocked on the door. The owner was awakened by the pecking sound and asked who it was, only to be told that it was a postman delivering a letter. He immediately ordered the servants to open the door and accept it. Unexpectedly, a total of four people rushed in. Realizing that he had been tricked by thieves, one of the thieves held an object resembling a pistol and prohibited anyone from making a sound, while the remaining thieves were about to search and rob. The cook in the house seized the opportunity to go outside and shout for thieves. The thieves did not dare to rob anything and fled, and the deputy police chief of the Jing'an Temple Police Station, McCloud, chased them to Avenue Avénue Edward VII, intercepted one of the thieves, and snatched the object he was holding, only to find that it was a screw. Two more thieves were subsequently captured, and after investigation by the First Special District Court, Meng Shousong, Mu Tingfu, and Jin Ayou were each sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment by Judge Feng yesterday.

Pushan Cemetery Charity Report 154

In April and May, the Pushan Cemetery buried a total of 520 large coffins and 4,466 small coffins of unclaimed bodies in the Chinese and foreign concessions. This included 222 large coffins and 2,097 small coffins received from the Municipal Council's various police stations and health departments for forensic examinations at various hospitals within the concession; 20 large coffins and 4 small coffins from the Tongde Baolong Laborers' Association and various Shanghai epidemic hospitals; 50 large coffins and 149 small coffins from the wartime refugee relief associations; 7 large coffins and 2 small coffins from the Chinese Red Cross Wounded Soldiers' Hospital; 2 large coffins and 28 small coffins from the Chinese Jisheng Association; 5 large coffins from the Lianyi Charity Association; 3 small coffins from the Red Swastika Society; 10 large coffins and 1 small coffin from the Shanghai Municipal Local Maintenance Committee; 6 large coffins and 30 small coffins from various hometown associations; 181 male and female bodies and 698 small coffins were collected by the cemetery's burial team in various places such as the Zhabei Great Field; 209 small coffins were collected from the Xiejiao branch; and 17 large coffins and 1,245 small coffins were sent by various charitable organizations. In total, 406 large coffins and 1,593 small coffins were distributed. The Xinmin and Pushan Hospitals provided free medical consultations and medicine to a total of 2,265 people.

World's Rare Gift 158

A book with signatures from 10,000 people of 50 nationalities, each using their own language, with illegible characters or fingerprints added, as a gift to congratulate the president of the Daidong Shipping Line and Wireless International Telegraph, Pan Daqun (J.C. Dinison Pendeis). Mr. Pan, feeling the world's economic panic, intends to adjust and maintain the company's foundation by trying to reduce the salaries of staff in various jurisdictions (saving 200,000 pounds annually from April to December). The 10,000 staff of 50 nationalities in various jurisdictions voluntarily sacrificed and supported this move, signing the book. It arrived in England on May 11th, which was Mr. Pan's 50th birthday. Mr. Pan was extremely pleased to receive this birthday gift of a book with signatures from 50 nationalities in various languages. At a time of economic exhaustion, this congratulation is also a special feature of the birthday gift.

Today, Mr. Zhang will still perform his lifetime masterpiece, the Frog Dance. Mr. Zhang has stopped performing this technique for seven years because it requires internal and external work and is very energy-consuming. For those who love to watch Mr. Zhang's martial arts but could not get tickets, today is the last chance.

Zhu Shengzai Loses Wife and Encounters Fraud 163

Angrily Reports to the Police Station

Yang Shepi and Others Detained

Zhu Shengzai, a 28-year-old Jiangxi native, has been running a palm mattress shop at 955 East-West Huade Road in the Public Concession. His wife, surnamed Wang, is an 18-year-old Cantonese woman with considerable beauty. On April 18th of this year, she suddenly went missing. Zhu searched everywhere, but to no avail. On the 24th, Yang Qiyuan (nickname "Shepi"), Ren Tianxing, Ren Yongxing, Ren Shunxiang, and others came, claiming, "We know your wife's whereabouts. If you want to see her again, you only need to give us 100 yuan as a gift, and we will forward it on your behalf." Zhu did not have this amount of money, but desperately missed his wife. He borrowed 10 yuan from his father, Lu Qifa, and handed it over to Yang Shepi at a small teahouse No. 53, Cangqiao Street, outside Xiaonanmen in the South City. Yang and the others then led Zhu to Zhang Yiben's place in Pudong. Zhang said to Zhu, "If you want your wife, that's easy. But you can't even scrape together a mere 'one-foot water head' (meaning 100 yuan). To be honest, people like us who 'eat the sun by day and drink the dew by night' don't have so much free time to deal with your petty affairs." Zhu had no choice but to return home and try to find a way, but he still couldn't raise the full amount. So, on the 4th of this month, he went to the South City again to plead with Yang, agreeing to pay the rest of the money after his wife was returned. Unexpectedly, Yang became furious upon hearing this, shouting loudly, "You are such an ungrateful person! We have been searching for your wife for you and have already spent a lot of money. Now, to be blunt, if you want your wife back, you must produce 140 silver dollars! Not even one copper coin less!" Zhu suspected that these people were intentionally extorting money. So, yesterday afternoon at about 4:00 PM, he reported the matter to the relevant section and precinct. The police were dispatched to the address, and Yang Shepi and the others were arrested. After being brought back, the precinct chief preliminarily questioned them and, considering the matter involved soliciting and extortion under false pretenses, and also suspected of abducting a married woman, ordered a written report to be submitted to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for thorough investigation.

Car Runs Over and Kills Child 164

Zhu Tugeng, a driver for the Paili Automobile Company, was driving car number 12660 at 12:25 PM on the 4th of this month, transporting passengers. While driving south on Avenue Saobao Sai in the French Concession, near Yufeng Lane, Chi Tongdeng, the six-year-old son of Chi Xuetang, the Shandong owner of the Hengtai Leather Shoe Store at number 132 on that road, was going out to buy something. He dashed out across the road from west to east. Zhu's car was unable to yield and struck Chi, injuring his head. The police recorded the license plate number and took the injured child, along with the car, to the police station, and then transferred him to the hospital. He died at 7:00 PM that night after treatment proved ineffective. The hospital notified the police station, who took the body to the Tongren Fuyuan branch hall for an autopsy. Yesterday morning, the vehicle affairs office summoned the family of the deceased, the defendant, and witnesses to the case, and reported it to the Second Special Court. Chen Beisan, the chief prosecutor, arrived at the scene and confirmed that the deceased had indeed died from a head injury caused by being struck by a car. He took his seat to formally hear the case, questioning the defendant and witnesses about the circumstances of the accident. He then ordered the body to be collected by the father of the deceased. The police station should investigate whether the defendant, Zhu Tugeng, was at fault and handle the matter according to the law.

Reconstruction of Sanlintang Completed 170

The streets of Sanlintang Township in Shanghai County had been in disrepair for many years and were extremely rugged. Last autumn, local gentry donated funds to rebuild them. This lasted for six months. Due to the impact of the war, work was suspended for two months. The project was completed yesterday. The road surface is entirely paved with crushed stone, with a length of 5,000 English feet and a width of 4 meters. The drainage cement ditch is 12 inches wide. The total cost of the project is more than 10,000 yuan.

Letters

To the editor, I recently read the solemn statement published in the news column of your newspaper on June 6th by the Postal Workers' Union, which stated that, according to reports, members Zhao Liancheng, Xing Rongzhao, Sun Hanliang, Tan Changde, and others violated public opinion and were instructed by a certain party to conspire to undermine the movement to consolidate the postal base. This is not in accordance with the facts. We are all members of the executive and supervisory committees of the union. We strongly support this postal workers' movement. However, the strike committee was manipulated by a minority of members of the union, and we, more than ten people who were obviously members of the action committee, were excluded. On June 3rd, at the general assembly, Zhu Xuefan and others reported and accused us of demanding a bribe of 30,000 yuan per person from the central government. The reporter, Yuan Shousheng, denied this. The details were published in your newspaper on June 6th as a warning. Such actions damage our personal reputation and dare to insult the central government. In addition to pursuing legal action, we request that your newspaper make a correction. We are sincerely grateful. Respectfully submitted to the Shen Bao Newspaper Office, Zhao Liancheng, Xing Rongzhao, Sun Hanliang, members of the executive committee, Tan Changde, member of the supervisory committee, Shanghai Postal Workers' Union. We respectfully request that your newspaper correct this to conform to the facts. We are sincerely grateful. Respectfully submitted to the editor of the Shen Bao Newspaper Office, the Chinese National Anti-Drug Association, June 6th.

Beijing Celebrates Teachers' Day 174

Nanjing, 6th. The Beijing Teachers' Day Commemorative Conference was held in the auditorium of Jinling University. Over 200 teachers from universities, middle schools, and primary schools attended. Order from the Jiangsu Education Department

Sincerely Instruct Students and Maintain School Spirit 175

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education issued an order to the heads of county education bureaus, stating that the incident in which the students of Xuzhou Middle School and Normal School went on strike and requested to be suspended as a whole because their request to visit other cities was not met has already been resolved by the department. All the causes and handling of the incident are understood. Although there are many reasons for the turmoil at the school, it must be recognized as a failure of moral education. Upon closer examination, it is related to the entire problem of school education. It cannot be solved by rectifying one school, nor can it be salvaged by punishing a few students, nor can it be fundamentally cleared by relying solely on severe measures. From the students' point of view, young people's blood is not yet settled, and they have not been deeply involved in the world. Their observation of things is easily confused by emotions. The occurrence of an incident inevitably involves many blind followers. By the time the situation has formed, those who handle it can only weigh the severity of the circumstances. How can they completely ignore the traces and return to the original intention? If they stumble one day, either their student status is removed, or their reputation is ruined, delaying their opportunity to study and losing their means of seeking knowledge is a small harm, but to cut off their ambition to learn and obliterate their conscience to repent, resulting in decadence and inaction for the rest of their lives, is a huge harm. Furthermore, they may be provoked to make a reckless decision. Once frustrated, they see themselves as no longer worthy of self-respect. Then, what cannot be done in terms of violating discipline and committing crimes? The impact is unimaginable. From the school's point of view, cultivating talent should create regular habits and a good environment to foster young people's self-governance and self-love. In terms of moral education on weekdays, it is necessary to influence them with sincerity and persuade them with reason. Once emotions are in harmony, reason will be easily guided. If, unfortunately, a conflict between teachers and students occurs, regardless of right or wrong, and regardless of how it is handled, discipline will be destroyed, and bad precedents will be created. The impact on the school's future is extremely significant. Even if it can be resolved quickly by following the law, the past wounds cannot be concealed, and subsequent remedies are even more difficult to achieve. Therefore, whether it is for the sake of the school, for the sake of the students, or even for the sake of the entire school education, in order to maintain school discipline, it is better to guide well at ordinary times than to punish after the event. To achieve students' academic success, it is better to prevent problems before they arise than to supervise after they have occurred. In the future, in addition to students following legal procedures to contribute reasonable opinions, the principals of each school should be open-minded, accept them, and implement them as appropriate. On weekdays, they must lead by example, work with all the teachers and staff to invigorate their spirits, and sincerely instruct them to ensure that all disputes are resolved invisibly, silently transformed, and integrated.

Reciprocally, so that the school does not damage its vitality, and the school spirit will gradually improve. If all efforts have been exhausted and the situation cannot be improved, and incidents still occur, the department will still adhere to the original policy and deal with them severely in order to treat both the symptoms and the root causes, and to be both lenient and strict. We will never be protective by condoning. This special order is for the bureau chiefs to forward to all concerned to comply with this order.

Local News

County Education Bureau

Promulgates Primary School Graduation Examination Measures 176

The Shanghai County Education Bureau has finalized the measures for this year's primary school graduation examination. Yesterday, it issued orders to each school to comply with them, and will supervise the students to wait for the test. The original order and measures are copied below. The order stated that the primary school graduation examination for this year has been determined and the date has been set. In addition to separate orders, the primary school graduation examination measures are copied and sent. The principals of each school shall comply and lead the sixth-grade students to the designated location at 9:00 AM on the specified date to wait for the bureau to send personnel to set the questions and test them. This is most important. The graduation examination measures are as follows: (1) Examination subjects: Party principles, Chinese, arithmetic, and general knowledge. (2) Examination locations: Except for Beiqiao Primary School, which will take the exam at Zhuanqiao Primary School, and the primary school attached to the Guangci Orphanage, which will take the exam at Minhang Central Primary School, the remaining schools, including Minhang Central, Qiangshu, Zhuanqiao, Tangwan, and Sanlin, will all be held at their respective schools. (3) Examination date: Starting at 9:00 AM on June 16th. (4) Examination time: 90 minutes for Chinese, 60 minutes for arithmetic, 40 minutes for general knowledge, and 40 minutes for party principles. (5) Lunch: Zhuanqiao Primary School should prepare meals or snacks for Beiqiao Primary School students (7 people) at a cost of no more than one dollar per person. No other schools will provide meals. (6) Graduation standards: Only those who pass both the school's own examination and the bureau's examination will be able to graduate. (7) Examination report: Each school shall prepare its own examination report for each subject (the size and style should be similar to the forms issued by the bureau), calculate the results, and report them to the bureau. The examination reports issued by the bureau should be filled out by each school with the names of the students taking the exam this year and handed over to the bureau's examiners on the examination date.

City ​​Lights,

Not a drop of oil.

Matches won’t light,

Big mouth cannot extinguish.

This lamp is wonderful. I really don't understand where the light comes from. That wire must be very important. Look, it is a double-stranded wire. There must be something wonderful about this strand. "Young Master Wu, why can't your light be blown out?" Young Master Wu laughed loudly in the living room and said: "You country bumpkin, this is an electric light, how can you blow it out? It's not difficult to make it turn dark. Look, it’s paired… isn’t it off? But on… interesting!” Chun Sheng also tried a few times. The more we tried, the more interesting it became, the more confused we became. Wu Dashao's half-baked explanation could not satisfy my desire for knowledge. I lay in bed and thought for a full hour and couldn't figure it out. In the end, I made a decision. Tomorrow I will hire a teacher. I can be content with his other qualifications, but if he can't tell me how the electric light emits light, I don't want to hire him. Yes, I must not forget to ask him why the people in those mirrors look so strange. If he can't explain this, he is not worthy to be the teacher of our ancient temple. Because if he can't answer these questions, what benefit will it bring to me, and what benefit will it bring to the children in our village? Haha, the teacher didn't test us, but we have to test the teacher first, how can this be! What other way do I have besides this?

A Prospect of the Tennis World 181

(Continued from yesterday)

Zheng Zhaojia Makes Rapid Progress Young tennis player Zheng Zhaojia is a proud student of Lin Baohua. In last year's Shanghai French Chamber of Commerce Hard Court Championships, veteran players Wit and Turk were defeated by Zheng, a young hero admired by the Chinese people. In the final against Canadian Davis Cup player De Fo, Zheng was defeated by De Fo, but the progress of his skills was truly astonishing. According to Lin, Zheng practices with James Potter at the school (John's University) court every day, and Lin gives him various strategies and points out errors every day. His skills have improved even more. Veteran hero Jiang Daozhang will likely concede defeat. According to Lin, if Zheng Zhaojia can maintain his current humble and eager-to-learn attitude, next year today, I (Lin Baohua) and Qiu Feihai may not be his match. Diligence leads to expertise. Zheng is truly a promising young man.

De Fo and Others Are Still in Shanghai Canadian Davis Cup player De Fo won the Shanghai Lawn Tennis Club's Open Singles and Hard Court Tennis Championships last year. In the semi-finals, he defeated Lin Baohua of China 3-1, and in the finals, he defeated Qiu Feihai, also by a score of 3-1. This man is still in Shanghai. Also, the Japanese player Hyosumi, who defeated Qiu Feihai last year, has not left Shanghai. These two are the big troubles for Lin and Qiu. However, this is enough to promote the vigilance and self-encouragement of our national players.

Lin Baohua Puts in Hard Work According to Lin himself, because De Fo and Hyosumi are in Shanghai, I must work hard to train from now on. I will never stop working hard, cut off social activities, study tennis, practice tennis, and pay attention to physical health to promote great fighting power, hoping to defeat De Fo and Hyosumi, restore the position of maritime leader, and intend to team up with Qiu Feihai to win the Robert Cup and Open Doubles championships. He hopes to go to the United States next year with Qiu Feihai and Zheng Zhaojia to represent China in the Davis Cup, to broaden their horizons and learn from each other, to promote China's interest in tennis and improve China's tennis level. The reporter believes that Lin's words show that he has not yet fulfilled his ambitions and deeply regrets it. Then, the people of the country should sincerely wish him well.

The United States Will Regain the Davis Cup The reporter also asked about the situation of this year's Davis Cup. Can the United States regain it from France? Lin replied that England will not do anything in this year's Davis Cup. The United States and France will meet again in George Town. The two American players, Vance and Hopkins, are very dangerous. The United States can definitely win the doubles, because Wenlein and Ellison are invincible in the world. Although France has the famous player Lacoste participating, Lacoste has retired for four years. Although he is making a comeback now, I am afraid he will not be able to restore his former glory. After this year's training, I know that he will definitely make great contributions to France next year. This year, Lacoste's participation in the Davis Cup may not be successful. As for Cochard, he has been prestigious for many years, but I am afraid he can only defeat the American Shields, but not Vance. Others, such as Borotra, are too old to fight for a long time. In short, the American Vance can win two singles, and Wenlein and Ellison win the doubles, then the United States will win the Davis Cup with a score of 3-2. However, the battle between the United States and France will take place in Paris. The French are accustomed to using Dunlop balls and hard courts, while the Americans are accustomed to using Tietelsen balls and grass courts. The elasticity of Dunlop balls is not as lively as that of Tietelsen balls, and balls on hard courts are difficult to catch. This is a major problem for the Americans. However, in order to regain the Davis Cup, the Americans are now instructing the Davis Cup players to gather in the western United States and practice on hard courts every day. If the United States regains the Davis Cup this year, it will be permanently displayed in the United States and will not be visited by other countries. This is due to the right time, the right place, and the right people. The reporter also deeply agrees with this statement. (The end)

The 10th World Olympic Games

Ambitions and Strength of Japanese Athletes (Part 2) Translated by Jiang Huaiqing 186

Are the Japanese Willing to Lag Behind? This World Olympic Games will be attended by 35 countries, with approximately 2,000 athletes gathering at the Olympic Arena in Los Angeles. Athletes from all countries are the best in the world at the moment, each striving with all their might and ability, hoping to win the championship, break records, and raise their respective national emblems in the joyful and enthusiastic international arena, in order to promote their international status. How can Japanese athletes allow athletes from other countries to take all the glory and willingly lag behind?

Substantial Strength. The grand and enthusiastic cheers and the melodious music will be broadcast from Los Angeles on Sunday, July 31st, at the opening ceremony of the 10th World Games. In this great gathering of famous athletes from around the world, there will be the Finnish middle and long-distance runner Paavo Nurmi, the 100-meter champion of the 9th World Games Percy Williams, the American sprint star Wykoff, and other equally strong athletic heroes from various countries, such as the American 1500-meter general Vansk, the sprint world's Torrence, the middle-distance's Istomen, and many famous players from Finland, Germany, and Sweden. In the previous Games, Japan ranked fifth in the track and field event, and this time they will definitely increase their strength, hoping to achieve the best results, and plan to send many female track and field athletes to participate.

A Sure Thing. There are a total of 30 Japanese track and field athletes participating, with the strongest strength in sprints, long jump, pole vault, and marathon running, and there will definitely be great success. Other events such as middle-distance running, hurdles, discus, javelin, and shot put may also have good results, and it is not difficult to gain a place in the Games. They are currently intensifying training and encouraging improvement, and their results will definitely be more impressive than before. Nambu Chuhei, a graduate of Keio University, created a world record of 7.98 meters in the long jump at the celebration sports meet at the Meiji Jingu Stadium in November last year. This result is difficult for athletes from various countries in modern times to match. In this World Games, Nambu is sure to win the long jump and triple jump championships. Others, such as Oshima Kamakichi of Kansai University, also have quite good jumping results.

Oda's Comeback. Oda Mikio, who created a new world record in the triple jump at the previous Dutch Games, originally planned to retire, but recently his ambition has revived, and he has made a comeback to win glory for Japan. He is currently training, and his triple jump results can still reach 15.70 meters, and his long jump can also reach 7.70 meters. If so, the long jump and triple jump in this Games will be dominated by Japan.

Sprints and Long Distance. Yoshioka Ryutoku, the leader of the Japanese sprint world, holds the Japanese record of 10.5 seconds in the 100 meters, and broke the Olympic Games record of 21.3 seconds in the 200 meters. When the American sprint star Simpson visited Japan last year, Simpson's 100 meters was also overwhelmed by Yoshioka, but the result was 10.7 seconds. In short, Yoshioka has great hope in the sprints at the 10th World Games. The national champion in long distance is Tsuda Seiichiro, also a graduate of Keio University. He holds the highest authority in races above 1,500 meters. Although he is now employed by an insurance company, he still works hard to train and spares no effort. His time for 1,500 meters is 4 minutes 3 seconds, and for 10,000 meters it is 32 minutes 4 seconds.

Marathon Long Run. Tsuda Seiichiro is also a famous marathon long-distance runner, invincible in Japan, and always wins the championship in every race. In the 1928 Dutch World Games, Tsuda Seiichiro, as a teenager, also won sixth place. Kamata Hisanosuke is also a marathon running expert in Japan. In the previous World Games, he had great hope of winning the championship. He was always in the lead within 24 miles, but unexpectedly, with only two miles remaining, both feet were injured and he could hardly move. However, he still endured the pain and struggled to win fourth place, with a time of 2 hours 35 minutes 29 seconds. Both of these people have great hope in this Games. (To be continued)

Free Talk

Sayings of the 93-Year-Old Ma Xiangbo

Reading Books Lighting Fire behind My Back 187

— Mei Hua

The first person to ask me to teach Latin was Liang Rengong. When Rengong asked me to teach him, he had already studied Latin for five months. Later, there were Cai Jimin, Zhang Jusheng, Wang Kangnian, and others. I was touched by the enthusiasm of these people for learning, and I thought of the general youth, so I decided to establish Aurora College.

The atmosphere of diligence in scholarship during the founding period of Aurora College was rare. At that time, the students not only had the ability to govern and motivate themselves, but also had a hundred times the courage to study, which was truly admirable! Sometimes I saw that they were working too hard, so I told them that they should rest, rest. Therefore, at that time, if students wanted to study, I would instead forbid them to study. At that time, oil lamps were still used at night. When I went to visit the students at night, everyone was reading under the lamp. When it was time to put out the fire, I personally went to put it out. After I left, they would light the fire again behind my back, which made it really impossible for me to deal with. Because they had such courage to study at that time, it was very strange that they could go on to read Latin anthologies after only five or six months of initial study. I once talked about this with foreigners, and they didn't believe it, thinking it was impossible. Later, Hu Dunfu went abroad to study in the United States. At that time, according to the American education system, one had to know Latin to enter university. Hu Dunfu said, "I have studied it in China." They didn't believe him, and took out a Latin anthology to test him on the spot. Coincidentally, the pages that were turned out were all what Hu Dunfu had studied at Aurora College. The test results showed that he could not only read but also explain, and then they were convinced.

After Reading "Letters from a Cottage" 188

— Han

My friend Xu Weinan told me that his friend Liu Dabai had died, "at a time when the country is in trouble and people are panic-stricken!"

Dabai once served as Deputy Minister of Education during Jiang Menglin's tenure as president. If he were a corrupt bureaucrat, his death would not be worth regretting. However, Dabai was a poet, a scholar, an educator, and one of the people I knew in my life who left a deep impression on me.

Six years ago, when I was the Director of General Affairs at Fudan University, Dabai and I lived in the South Dormitory. I lived in the southernmost room, and he lived in the northernmost room. He was in charge of academic affairs, and I was in charge of general affairs, so naturally we had few opportunities to talk. However, my impression of him was very deep. I heard that Dabai's funeral was poor, and the quilt in the coffin covered his head but not his feet. Before his death, he mentioned wanting to talk to a few friends about his funeral arrangements, but finally sighed and said, "My friends are all poor friends with pens, so there's no need to talk about the funeral!"

Weinan was Dabai's confidant. Since Dabai's death, the famous humorist Weinan has also become a "mourning family member." In order to commemorate Dabai and to help with the education of Dabai's children, he specially took out the letters Dabai wrote to him. There were a total of eighty letters, compiled into "Letters from a Cottage." "From these eighty letters, we can at least catch a glimpse of Dabai's personality, learning, life, hopes, and his illness."

I know Dabai to some extent, so I finished reading "Letters from a Cottage" in one breath. I think this little book is indeed worth recommending, especially to young friends, who should all read this book.

There are many wonderful things in "Letters from a Cottage." Let me excerpt a few passages to offer to the readers:

Han Palace Spring 189

— Lao Lan

My family's Hai Shan Xian Hall. Located in Ban Tang Litchi. It is the old site of the Changhua Garden of the Southern Han Dynasty. The other residence of my paternal uncle, Duke Deyu of Fangbo. Waterside pavilion and wind corridor. Stretching for dozens of miles. There is a Bi Huang in the middle. It imitates the Three Pools Mirroring the Moon in West Lake. Seven ponds are opened to form it. My footprints have covered Wu and Yue. I have seen the Inner Garden Kunming Lake. The so-called famous gardens. I have not been able to compare. Now people and things have changed. Time has changed the scenery. Leaning on the boat and gazing. Only a hundred acres of fragrant pond remain. Lotus flowers send the evening. The picture painted by Xia Mingzhi and Tian Shiyou. Still in a friend's house. Sometimes I borrow it for browsing. You can still point out one or two of its grand aspects. In the summer of Xin Wei. Occasionally missing my hometown. I wrote this tune.

Scattered sacred mountains. Recognize the old site of Changhua. Bay of Dan Litchi. The green lotus of the desolate pond rises late. New formation in the summer. The moon is reflected in the Three Pools. Compared to West Lake. The tide is calm and the wind is gentle. All have been changed. Broken bridge and abandoned hall. All plans to clean up Fangzhou. Looking back at the sea and mulberry fields becoming illusions. Even the Qi Yun is tied with brocade. How many times have I come to visit. Old mansions in black clothes. Give way to the occasional seagulls. Golden titles and brocade brocade. There are people who embroider.

People have left their names in the books. I am old. Will Qing Ban be done? Returning home to reorganize the fishing boat.

"The three things that have influenced me most in my life are the eight-legged essay, mathematics, and Buddhist scriptures. Mathematics has cultivated a more logical mind in me, and Buddhist scriptures have cultivated my sense of sacrifice and courage. As for the eight-legged essay, it should have given me a bad influence... but I got from it a relatively meticulous exercise of my mind. What I also got from the Buddhist scriptures is the universal love of religion." From this fragment, we can see the foundation of Dabai's outlook on life.

Dabai didn't want to be an official but became an official, so he often complained to Weinan. The redder his official position became, the more intense his complaints became:

"This kind of life, which is based on circumstances, has been going on for almost ten months. There is no joy of music, but the labor of documents. You think how dry this is, but I am not afraid of this; what I am most afraid of is the siege of the rice bowl party."

"Now you should congratulate me. Old Liu's official luck is not higher than a hot air balloon but thinner than a hot air balloon, this hot air balloon has already burst!"

Dabai's advice to Weinan is worth its weight in gold and can serve as a guide for young people to live and conduct themselves in the world. Let me quote a passage from "Letters from a Cottage":

"People often say that you should have a long-term vision; it is true that you cannot do without a long-term vision. However, if your vision is too long-term, you will not see the practical problems in front of you.

"When people do things, they must be tempered by dealing with the smallest and most difficult practical problems."

There are really too many wonderful aphorisms in "Letters from a Cottage." I would still like to ask the readers to buy the original book and read it. (Note: This book is sold by Shanghai and other World Book Company branches, priced at three corners.) (Remuneration is donated to the Liu family's orphans)

A Record of the Exhibition of Cultural Relics of the Qi Yang Family (Part 1) 190

— K

The Exhibition of Cultural Relics of the Qi Yang Family, hosted by Zhu Qiqian (Gui Xin), was held at Zhongshan Park in Beiping from 3:00 PM to 5:00 PM on May 23rd. Zhang Hanqing, Chen Renxian, Jiang Menglin, and other gentlemen and ladies, numbering over a hundred, visited one after another. After the flowers in the park had faded, it was a temporary success. The cultural relics were displayed in two rooms, totaling fifty-six items. Qu Guanying, Yuan Tongli, Qiu Meizhi, Liang Sicheng, and others assisted in organizing, collating, and displaying them. Starting from the 24th, it will be open to the public for two weeks. Among them, such items as the ink edict of Emperor Taizu of Ming and the Picture of the Li Clan Pacifying the Barbarians can all be used as factual evidence for the history of the Ming Dynasty, which is of great benefit to scholarship and is by no means superficial. Zhu told reporters that if people from the South are willing to study, they only need to provide a suitable display location, and he would be happy to promote culture.

The Beiping Society for Research in Chinese Architecture has compiled a special book on the examination of cultural relics of the Qi Yang family, which is difficult to transcribe one by one. Here are the main points:

Modern Chinese historical materials hidden in family histories are extremely abundant. However, after so many tribulations, there are not many that still have their brilliance. Only the Qi Yang family has maintained its continuity for more than 600 years.

On Frugality and Thrift to Save the Nation (4) 191

— Narrated by Nie Zengjifen, Written by her Son Qi Jie

Its influence extends to the social economy. Everything is chosen from the West instead of the Chinese. China's old crafts are gradually being eliminated, and the number of unemployed and impoverished people has increased. Last year, the value of imported goods was a huge amount of 220 million yuan, with a deficit of 80 million yuan. This is the obvious effect of promoting European trends and developing desires in recent years. It's like a patient, further injured, bleeding non-stop. How can one expect them to live long? Today, people often say that this is the fault of capitalist aggression by imperialists. That's true. However, isn't Japan in the same position, equally subjected to capitalist aggression by European and American countries? Why is it that they can consolidate and strengthen themselves, and are so feared by the powers? The inconvenience of daily life and clothing is most evident in Japan. If Japan also competed in luxury, sought convenience, and sought comfort, then they would inevitably abandon what they already had and seek it externally. The huge amount of money spent would be unimaginable. Items such as Western-style bathtubs, toilets, stoves, wardrobes, iron beds, coil spring mattresses, tables, chairs, carpets, etc., are all considered indispensable by new Chinese figures. However, in that country, except for a very small number of noble families and wealthy merchants and public buildings, ordinary middle-class families generally do not have such things. Ordinary houses do not even have glass windows. The fact that the majority of their people can resolutely adhere to their old customs and be content with inconvenience and discomfort is because they can restrain their private desires in order to preserve the spirit and material resources of the nation. This cannot be achieved without the power of education, and the reason why their educators were able to have this foresight decades ago is because the reformers at that time were deeply indebted to Chinese scholarship (mostly Yangming scholars). They were able to see far and wide, knowing that preserving the national essence is the way to strengthen the nation's power, so they were not invaded by Western culture. Rituals and frugality are the beautiful essence of Chinese culture. Rituals are based on self-restraint and desire control. Less desire leads to order and frugality. This is what people today criticize as passive morality and cannibalistic rituals, so they do the opposite and say, "Developing desires can promote culture." Alas, what do the facts prove? Throughout history, all those who have been able to benefit their people and benefit their country, as evidenced by historical records, are rich in this passive morality.

Replacing it is a historical trace. The Qi Yang family is Li Wenzhong, the nephew of Emperor Taizu of Ming, who followed Emperor Taizu to rise up in the army, establish meritorious service, and establish the country. Wenzhong's son, Jinglong, participated in the Jingnan Campaign. Later, he was convicted and imprisoned. He was pardoned and re-enfeoffed during the Hongzhi reign. During the Wanli reign, his descendant, Zongcheng, served as the Japanese envoy. After the fall of the Ming Dynasty, his descendants joined the banner system and settled in Beidu. They continued to be prominent in literature and officialdom until today. Although they have been reduced to commoners in the former capital, they still carefully adhere to their old possessions. Among this collection of old possessions, there is the ink edict given by Emperor Mingzu, clothing worn by him, portraits of emperors of past generations, and illustrated books of meritorious deeds. The historical materials are precious and can be considered first-class.

A Brief Record of Visiting a Refugee Factory 192

— Xu Wancheng

The Japanese army bombed Shanghai, wantonly slaughtering innocent civilians in Zhabei, Jiangwan, Taicang, and Changshu. Shops, factories, markets, and houses were all destroyed! The cries of the wounded were everywhere, people were displaced, and the number of homeless people totaled more than 100,000. Who is to blame? Who caused this? It is truly heart-wrenching!

Comrades from the People's Livelihood Improvement Society, Huang Jingxiang, Pan Yangyao, Ying Shugui, Li Denghui, and others formed a subcommittee to discuss the issue of refugees' livelihoods. Chaired by Huang, they established the "January 28th Refugee Factory." Funding was temporarily provided by the Chinese Christian Church and several national entities and private individuals. The factory site is located on Luo Beigen Road in Beixinjing. I visited yesterday and made the following notes:

The factory initially accommodated more than 90 refugees, and more are being admitted. All have work. The elderly and weak are assigned to watch the gate, help raise children, and twist ropes, while the young and strong are learning a skill, each with a master to teach them. Children of school age are sent to school. Refugee workers also have night school classes in the evenings, all managed by Ms. Bai Zhian. Refugees live naturally. Mothers and daughters, husbands and wives, fathers and sons, and brothers who have family organizations can still live together, while widowers and single women are separated. The factory is temporarily divided into (A) Sock Factory, (B) Rattan Factory, (C) Wood Factory, (D) Tailoring, and (E) Straw Factory. In addition, it is planned to add "Weaving," "Leather," and "Glass" departments. According to Huang, "Refugees are not easy to train. Disputes often occur. They are greedy, lazy, and unwilling to work. Sincere guidance is needed."

After refugees enter the factory, they are trained in a craft by a master according to their personality and interests, implementing the principle of "working to eat." The factory plans to rename itself "Cooperative Factory" in the future. Its purpose is to help suffering compatriots, not to be compared with capitalist-invested factories. The surplus of labor is still consumed by the laborers. The future development of the factory will be the center of the Beixinjing district. Huang hopes to deeply involve the people and engage in rural reconstruction movements.

The Tale of the Prosperous Horse Double Residence (71) 193

— Owner of the Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter 9: With a Special Train, Chasing Away Guests with False Alarms; Sitting in a Cold Government Office, Turning into Stone with Longing. Mao Deshun quietly pushed An Yutian from behind. An Yutian also immediately understood that this seat could not tolerate his presumptuous occupation for long. He got up to say goodbye, vacating the good position near the water pavilion, allowing those with sufficient status to accompany the commander-in-chief. However, he was already very satisfied. He retreated to the fifth wife's compartment, where he was asked by Liang Xiaoyun and briefly reported some of the satisfying experiences. He thanked the fifth wife again for her thoughtful care. Liang Xiaoyun was delighted. He also sat heavily, carefully organizing and recalling the various impressions he had just gained. Among these, what he found most peculiar was that Ye Zuozhang was not as crude as he had imagined, nor as bad as the public opinion attacked him to be. A crude person could not have said so many reasonable things. An evil person, in particular, would not have been so eager to use talent. It can be seen that a military man being able to reach such a high position as a military governor was by no means entirely due to luck. He must have had his own strengths. One does not know until one has experienced it. Hearing is not as good as seeing. He had been holding on to the views of a scholar, dismissing such warlords in general, which was a mistake. However, the mistakes were increasing, and he had been bewitched by the warlords, poisoned by the warlords, and was truly about to surrender willingly, beyond help. Thinking randomly in this way, he vaguely passed by this good show, seeing without seeing and hearing without hearing. The couple then personally sent the fifth wife back to the residence, where the fifth wife invited them to come in and talk for a while. They talked about inviting them both to take the special train to Beijing. Before leaving, they could come here to board the train together, and she would send someone to take care of everything. Liang Xiaoyun thought that since her husband was going out to work for the first time, she, as his virtuous assistant, had to assist him in every way. If she was often with the fifth wife, she could also hold on to this powerful internal connection. She immediately agreed with joy. After leaving the Ye residence and returning home, the couple again discussed finishing up matters at the Beijing residence. Many bulky chests and wooden furniture were inconvenient to carry because this time they were riding on someone else's special train. Also, the matter had not been fully settled, so they could not rashly move the whole family. They had to temporarily leave it in Beijing. The chests were locked and sealed, and all the wooden furniture and sundries were locked in the various rooms, leaving the tenant Chang Sheng and the nanny A Jin to guard them. The couple only brought some clothes to change, packed in two or three small, convenient leather bags. They took along the servant Wang Ding and a young maid, A Qiao. They also withdrew a sum of money from the bank and opened a draft, specifically for this trip's expenses.

Futures trading, however, far surpassed the previous day, with significant price drops on the market, leading to a sudden increase in market activity. Among these, the Supervisory Tax accounted for 1.185 million yuan, the Consolidated Tax accounted for 900,000 yuan, the 20 Customs bonds and troop disbandment bonds each accounted for over 700,000 yuan, and other bonds accounted for 3-400,000 yuan. The 96 Customs bonds still had the May contract, with only the Feng Tax opening at 15,000 yuan. The changes were primarily due to rumors of the Minister of Finance's resignation, creating a sense of weakness, leading to increased selling pressure and significant price declines. However, as each price dropped sharply in the early morning, and investment interest remained strong, the supply and demand situation did not change significantly, so the price fluctuated without large increases or decreases. As a result, prices fell by 6-7 jiao to around 1.5 yuan compared to the previous day. In general, the market situation for bonds was still relatively good.

Silk and Tea

Haiment New Cocoon Harvest Also Poor 205

Purely Damaged by Weather... Total Harvest Less Than 30%

The farmers in the coastal sandbanks of Haimen who raised spring silkworms this year only accounted for 50% of last year. There were different types of silkworm eggs, and few stable foreign varieties were hatched. Most used self-retained local varieties for hatching. Due to unfavorable weather, the extent of damage to silkworm larvae reached 60%. The loss of silkworm production was less than 30% of the total harvest. Farmers suffered unrecoverable losses on their silkworm investment. The new cocoons have already been launched on the market. Only three or four silk merchants have opened for business. The initial price for local cocoons was only 15-16 yuan. Improved cocoons rose to 20 yuan. Most of the local cocoons are of inferior quality with thin shells, and silk merchants are refusing to weigh and collect them.

Both Arrivals and Sales of Red and Green Tea are Strong 206

Yesterday, over 8,300 boxes of silk and tea from Tunxi, Shexian, and other routes, and black tea from Qimen and Fuliang routes, arrived in Shanghai. Among tea transactions, Qimen tea was still the most popular, but there were many second and third batches of goods with inferior quality, selling for 80-90 taels, unchanged from last week. Merchants such as Yingzhuang, Jinlong, Yihua, and Tianyu from Tunxi and Shexian all had a good appetite for Zhenmei tea. The market was especially active for Zhenmei tea. Top-grade goods from Tunxi opened as high as 80 taels, and sales were extremely strong. The sales of Pingshui pearl tea to the U.S. have also become active. However, due to telegrams from New York indicating low prices, Chinese tea merchants are mostly unwilling to compromise and sell off their stock due to cost considerations.

Wuyuan Tea Merchants Stop Making Top-Grade Sprout Tea 207

After searching for new tea leaves for the past ten days, tea merchants in Wuyuan have sold 60-70% of their inventory in the market. As a result, the asking price in recent days has only dropped by 3-4 yuan compared to before. Mountain households are not worried about unsold inventory due to the limited stock, and the mood is very stable. In view of the recent sluggish Shanghai market and the fact that sales prices are not as good as in previous years, tea merchants mostly intend to temporarily purchase one batch and then observe the market trend before deciding whether to add more stock. The past two days, Yi Zhuang has repeatedly received telegrams from Shanghai stating that the opening price for Tunzhen is 155, but there were no further negotiations, and the merchants stopped making bud core tea, etc. Upon receiving this news, the tea merchants became even more cautious and reduced costs in line with market trends. They all made less bud core tea and switched to making regular Zhenmei tea to avoid heavy losses. The top-grade bud core vanilla and Longteng Wanli Donglu goods from Jinzhu Jitai Tea House are all being shipped from Hangzhou to Shanghai and are expected to arrive in Shanghai around the beginning of the month to show samples.

Fuliang Green Tea Prices and Sales Fall Slightly 208

Ten days ago, merchants from the Xiuning and Wuyuan regions flocked to buy Fuliang's southeastern green tea, and mountain households took advantage of the situation to raise prices. Market prices once rose to over 60 yuan. About 50% of the tea in the mountains has been sold. Now, due to the sluggish Shanghai market, the merchants from Xiuning and Wuyuan are abandoning the purchase of tea with inferior water leaves compared to their own tea gardens. Even if there is a need, the prices must be reduced by 30 yuan. As a result, general merchants who wanted to wait for higher prices are unable to sell their unsold inventory and are very anxious. Therefore, the market price for Fuliang tea has not only fallen but also there are very few inquiries.

Commentary

The Issue of Restoring Diplomatic Relations with the Soviet Union 218

— Fo

Newspapers advocating and opposing the restoration of diplomatic relations with the Soviet Union are engaged in a fierce war of words, exchanging blows and kicks. However, Japan, without making a sound, has already been secretly negotiating with Soviet Russia and is close to success.

According to foreign news yesterday, Japan is not rushing on the Northeast issue, not because it fears the investigation team, but to divide the spoils with Russia. It is also rumored that Japan will temporarily stay out of the limelight and have the puppet government of the Northeast first enter into a restoration of diplomatic relations with Russia, including the exchange of envoys and consuls. Europe and the United States are paying close attention to this matter. If this news is confirmed, then both those advocating and opposing the restoration of diplomatic relations with the Soviet Union are making much ado about nothing.

Today, let me tell a joke. Two people, A and B, both nearsighted, are competing with each other and cannot resolve their dispute. C says, "Tomorrow, a new plaque will be hung in a certain temple, and you can test your eyesight." A and B are both cunning. A first goes to eavesdrop on the four large characters on the plaque. B is even more cunning and inquires about the inscription above and below.

The next day, the two go together. A points to the plaque in the hall and says, "The four characters are such and such." B says, "The large characters are easy to recognize. I can also identify the inscription." The two start arguing again, accusing each other of eavesdropping. Just then, the temple monk comes out from inside and asks what they are arguing about. The two tell him the story. The monk laughs and says, "Gentlemen, please do not argue. The plaque is still in the back room and has not been hung yet." The two return in embarrassment.

Gentlemen, you are drawing your swords, ready to strike, faces red with anger, arguing vehemently. Aren't you similar to them?

Literature

Slow Tune: Yangzhou — Passing Zhabei 219

— Chen Jiaqing

The prosperity of Shanghai, the beauty of Jiangnan, spring breezes cause sorrow overnight. Look, the ashes of the disaster are everywhere, all turned into ruined cities. I remember the spring scenery filled my eyes, the reds and greens were intoxicating, and singing and dancing prevailed. But now, dry wells and dilapidated walls evoke boundless sadness.

Our great rivers and mountains are carelessly abandoned, causing alarm. Alas, drinking the blood of the Xiongnu, devouring the flesh of the foreign invaders, one basket of earth completes the task. A million soldiers are still there; don't laugh, wait for the snail's fight. I think of the capital, thousands of miles away, where the mournful sound of the horns is not heard.

Helping each other late, meeting is also fate. Just awakened from a dream, I boarded the boat. Going west, the soldiers are numerous; coming east, the scenery is changing. At night, we talked about national affairs, but I dared not speak in front of others.

Science

Classification of Rubber Product Manufacturing Methods and Overview of Factories in China 221

— Shen Zhibin

Rubber Overview. This supplement already has a considerable introduction, but the actual working conditions of the factory and the types of manufacturing methods, and the development of this career in China, are probably also something readers are pleased to hear, so I will briefly describe the services I have received, as follows:

Rubber has been valued by the world for its vulcanization method, so its manufacturing method is to add sulfur and make it work. However, there are various working methods, and those that have been used in factories can actually be simply divided into four categories:

(1) Hot Vulcanization Method: Many products are made by this method, and it is impossible to list them all. The working steps are to mix rubber with compounding agents, and then add sublimated sulfur, fully mixed in a mixing machine, rolled into a plate shape, formed into goods, and sent to a heater for oxidation. However, there are many types of heaters and methods, such as "direct hot vulcanization". Representative products include shoe heels and rubber bricks. However, this method is too old and is rarely used now. "Direct steam vulcanization" In addition to heating, mixed rubber products also need to be pressurized. This method is very advantageous for products because of the steam pressure. However, those with surface color relationships are not applicable. "Indirect steam vulcanization" There are many different forms of this device, but its principle is to pass steam through a snake tube and heat it in a secret chamber or container, but there is only heat and no pressure, and there are many shortcomings. However, engineers can still remedy it with appropriate drugs, depending on whether the engineer can use it. "Indirect steam pressure vulcanization" This method uses an air pump machine to increase air pressure, or a press in a compressor. Many factories are using it now. In addition, there are those who use electric heat instead of steam heat, but because the cost is higher, there are few users. Most of the methods used by various factories in China are hot vulcanization methods.

(2) Cold Vulcanization Method: This method uses green gas and sulfur compounds to complete the vulcanization and oxidation process at room temperature. I have not heard of any factories in China using this method to make products. Products should be thin sheets, such as medical equipment, children's toys, and rubber gloves, all of which can be vulcanized by this method. There are also those who use both cold and hot methods to make products such as raincoats.

(3) Air Vulcanization Method: This method also has two types, one is a variation of hot vulcanization, and the other is a variation of cold vulcanization. The former melts sulfur in a container, unlike the hot vulcanization method, which uses sulfur mixed with products. The United States calls this method the sulfur mine bath method, because the products are bathed in sulfur air. The latter sends a recorded sulfur compound gas into a secret chamber where the products have been placed to complete the vulcanization work. There are many products such as gloves, hot water bags, diving caps, and life buoys, and the properties are better than those made by the cold vulcanization method, because cold vulcanized products are slightly weaker in toughness and tensile force.

(4) High-Pressure Heavy Heat Vulcanization Method: This method requires that the rubber be turned into a solid, and 2-3% of sulfur iodine must be added, and it must be oxidized under high pressure and heat for a long time, and the coordination method is also very important. Usually high-grade oil wax is used to help it be dense and smooth. The finished product is commonly called Bakelite. It has insulation and is used for electrical material decorations, records, and fountain pen shafts, but if the manufacturing method is poor, it will soften when exposed to heat.

The history of China's rubber chemical industry is less than 100 years. Most of the products are made by the hot vulcanization method, and shoes are the most famous. Other things still need to be revitalized, so the level is actually very childish. Because the country is restless, the asset class is always less interested in industry, and there is a great shortage of technical personnel. There are often cases of hiring foreign technicians, so technology cannot be improved through research, and engineering power is controlled by others, and domestic raw materials cannot be used. Among the raw materials, there are many natural raw materials in China such as zinc oxide, lead oxide, calcium carbonate, magnesium carbonate, chalk, and all special rubber oil agents, rubber substitutes, etc., which can be easily chemically made. It is a pity that Chinese people do not research or have little transportation, and capitalists are superstitious in foreigners, and the power of profit overflows, which is regrettable.

Literary Anecdotes

Meeting 222

— Lu Dan

(1)

On the bulletin board were pasted various notices of different sizes, colors, and fonts, all with the same (or similar) message:

"This association will hold its nth regular meeting on the nth day of the month at the nth hour in classroom nth. All members are requested to attend." [Name of Association, Date]

There are at least three to five gatherings every day. Some are alumni associations, some are student associations, and there are also various societies and groups. Anyway, as long as there are people, there is a name. College students have plenty of money and time, so why not be "active"?

(2)

Several young ladies were sitting in the shade of a tree, causing the gentleman who was recruiting people for the meeting to sweat profusely. I saw him put on a solemn expression, trying to suppress his nervous mood, and said to Ms. A, who was known as an activist:

"Ms. A, please go to classroom X to attend the meeting." He seemed both relieved and resentful. Ms. A muttered to herself as she got up:

"It's really tiring to call people to meetings every day." Indeed, Ms. A is very hardworking. Her name is always on the list of officers in every association.

(3)

The W Society was holding an executive committee meeting. The male executives had all arrived, but Ms. C was still late. The chairman pleaded repeatedly, and everyone agreed to wait. However, when the chairman returned from the fourth invitation, he reported:

"Ms. O hasn't finished her hair yet and probably can't come to the meeting..."

"Why do women automatically give up their due rights?" This was the voice of a sentimentalist.

This meeting seemed to pass in a spiritless manner.

Sexual Issues

Conditions for Seeking Love 223

— A Niu

I often see couples of men and women walking hand in hand in the park and on the road, whispering endless sweet words. But after careful examination of their results, although I don't have precise statistics, the end result is often a tragic comedy in which they break up and hire lawyers to go to court. Why? Because they don't meet the following six conditions.

The first condition: if you want to seek a beautiful lover, then ask yourself, how much property do you have? Or how much income do you have each month? Is it enough for your lover to buy long stockings, high-heeled leather shoes, cheongsams, dance dresses, French cosmetics, and all kinds of miscellaneous expenses?

The second condition: do you have a western-style house and a car? Of course! How can a lover as beautiful as a peach blossom and as lovely as jade be crowded into a low bungalow and lightly move her jade feet to run on the road? So you have to prepare an exquisite western-style house where you can hide your beauty, and a new-style car where you can take a joyride or drive to the dance floor.

The third condition: what is your own or your father's or brother's position in society? Are you a highly respected PhD, master, expert, or even a chairman, president, or minister in the national government, or a mayor in a city, a county magistrate in a county, or a commander-in-chief, army commander, division commander, brigade commander, or regiment commander holding a gun?

The fourth condition: what is your appearance? First, you have to take a mirror and look at yourself. If you can pass the test, then there is no problem. If you are very ugly or have a face full of freckles, then a weasel can't eat swan meat.

The fifth condition: what is your level of education? If you are a middle school student, then don't think about finding a college student as a lover. You can only find an elementary school graduate. If you are a college student, you can only pair with a middle school student. If you are a PhD or master who has returned from studying abroad, then you can pick any college student you want. If you are only an elementary school graduate, then you can only pick an illiterate person who has not studied.

The sixth condition: do you have a slavish nature? Are you willing to be at your lover's beck and call? If you don't have any of the above six conditions, then no matter how hard you try, the arrow of love will not visit you. Even if it does, you will not enjoy your blessings forever.

But what about these Misses? I say, please rest assured! As long as you put on a few layers of rouge and powder, someone will come after you.

Business Economics

Fortune Teller 224

— Yi

I remember when I was working at the Kunshan XX Central Elementary School, one afternoon after class, a dozen colleagues who lived at school were gathered in a corner of the playground, chatting and laughing. A tinkling bell sound reached our ears. I walked out of the school gate and saw that it was a fortune teller. From a distance, what made us laugh the most was his appearance, so we called him in. He was a middle-aged man in his thirties, with a sallow face and black teeth, obviously an opium addict. He wore a white bamboo cloth long shirt that was as dirty as a tablecloth, and he was dragging a pair of broken black cloth shoes. In his hand, he carried a large British brand cigarette box. Inside the box, of course, were the tools he used to cheat people out of food. After he sat down, he opened his treasure chest.

"What kind of character?"

"I dropped a fountain pen. I don't know if I can find it." I put on a solemn expression and told him seriously. My colleagues all thought it was a serious matter and watched. "Oh, how many days ago did you drop it?"

"More than a week ago."

"Bring out a piece of paper!" Hao casually grabbed one and opened it. It was the character "木" (wood). He began to expound his theory, determining that it could not be found. Hao suddenly laughed and took out his good old Parker from his pocket and said, "I didn't drop it..." The fortune teller's face turned red immediately. We also touched our heads and laughed loudly, clapping our hands and stomping our feet. Finding himself in a dead end, the fortune teller stood up, bowed to us, and began to recount his experiences. "To be honest with you gentlemen, I am a normal school graduate. I have been a primary school teacher for several years. It was my own fault that I got addicted to opium. My family property was used up, and I couldn't be a teacher anymore. There was really no way, so I had to resort to this tactic. I hope you gentlemen will forgive my suffering..." As he spoke, he expressed infinite pain. We were also stunned by his words for a long time.

Reply Letter 225

Reply Letter to Mr. Gong,

Respectfully, yesterday I happened to read this newspaper and saw the inquiries from Mr. Tang and Mr. Yang regarding my business. Now I respectfully answer as follows. Mr. Tang's inquiries regarding "direct, spicy, Nikahn oil, etc." can be purchased at all chemical industrial raw material stores (such as the Practical Learning and Art Hall and the Scientific Instrument Hall on Chessboard Street). The prices vary with time, and each store also has ups and downs, so it is not convenient to inform in detail. Please inquire at each store yourself.

Mr. Yang's inquiry about sodium chloride can also be purchased from the stores listed above. As for how much warm water to use for one ounce of sodium chloride, it is related to the temperature of the water in which the sodium chloride is dissolved. If the temperature is high, less water is needed, so please use your discretion. Dissolving sodium chloride in water will absolutely not cause an explosion or danger.

Respectfully, Gong.

School students are given special discounts, and they can enjoy an 80% discount to encourage interest in studying electrical engineering.
